### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Arquitetura de Referência

## 1. Estrutura do Projeto V12

```
diyapp-v12/
├── src/
│   ├── core/
│   │   ├── agents/           # Agentes autônomos
│   │   │   ├── tech-lead/
│   │   │   ├── code-reviewer/
│   │   │   ├── security-specialist/
│   │   │   └── llm-specialist/
│   │   ├── orchestrator/     # Orquestração de agentes
│   │   ├── memory/           # Sistema de memória persistente
│   │   ├── monitoring/       # Monitoramento e métricas
│   │   └── api/             # APIs internas

└── config/
    ├── development.yaml
    ├── staging.yaml
    └── production.yaml
```

## 2. ADR-001: Arquitetura de Agentes Autônomos

**ADR-001: Arquitetura Baseada em Agentes Autônomos com Memória Persistente**

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead, LLM Specialist

**CONTEXTO:**
Precisamos de uma arquitetura que suporte múltiplos agentes especializados trabalhando em paralelo no Modo Hive, com comunicação assíncrona e memória persistente para aprendizado contínuo.

**DECISÃO:**
Implementar arquitetura baseada em agentes autônomos com:
1. Sistema de mensagens pub/sub para comunicação entre agentes
2. Banco de dados vetorial para memória de longo prazo
3. Sistema de orquestração centralizado com fallback distribuído
4. Monitoramento em tempo real de todos os agentes

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**
- **Opção A:** Arquitetura monolítica tradicional
  - Prós: Simples de desenvolver, debugging fácil
  - Contras: Escalabilidade limitada, single point of failure
- **Opção B:** Microserviços completos
  - Prós: Alta escalabilidade, isolamento de falhas
  - Contras: Complexidade operacional, overhead de comunicação
- **Opção C:** Agentes autônomos com orquestração leve
  - Prós: Balanceamento ideal, resiliência, paralelismo natural
  - Contras: Complexidade inicial de implementação

**Opção escolhida: C** — Justificativa: Melhor equilíbrio entre autonomia e coordenação, ideal para Modo Hive.

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
**Positivas:**
- Paralelização natural de tarefas
- Resiliência a falhas individuais
- Escalabilidade horizontal fácil
- Isolamento de responsabilidades

**Negativas:**
- Complexidade aumentada de debugging
- Overhead de comunicação entre agentes
- Necessidade de sistema de orquestração robusto

**Riscos:**
- Deadlocks em comunicação entre agentes
- Consistência de dados entre agentes
- Mitigação: Timeouts configuráveis, transações distribuídas

**REVISÃO:** 2024-04-15

## 3. Engineering Standards V12

```typescript
// src/shared/types/engineering-standards.ts

export const EngineeringStandards = {
  // Padrões de Código
  code: {
    language: 'TypeScript',
    version: '5.0+',
    styleGuide: {
      naming: {
        variables: 'camelCase',
        constants: 'UPPER_SNAKE_CASE',
        classes: 'PascalCase',
        interfaces: 'I{PascalCase}',
        files: 'kebab-case',
      },
      formatting: {
        indent: 2,
        maxLineLength: 100,
        quotes: 'single',
        semi: true,
      },
    },
    testing: {
      framework: 'Jest',
      coverage: {
        minimum: 80,
        goal: 90,
        branches: 75,
        functions: 80,
        lines: 80,
        statements: 80,
      },
      patterns: {
        unit: '*.test.ts',
        integration: '*.integration.test.ts',
        e2e: '*.e2e.test.ts',
      },
    },
  },

  // Padrões de Git
  git: {
    branching: {
      strategy: 'GitFlow',
      branches: {
        main: 'production',
        develop: 'integration',
        feature: 'feature/*',
        hotfix: 'hotfix/*',
        release: 'release/*',
      },
    },
    commits: {
      convention: 'Conventional Commits',
      types: ['feat', 'fix', 'docs', 'style', 'refactor', 'test', 'chore'],
      scopeRequired: true,
    },
    pullRequests: {
      minimumApprovals: 2,
      requiredChecks: ['lint', 'test', 'build', 'security-scan'],
      sizeLimit: 400,
    },
  },

  // Padrões de API
  api: {
    versioning: 'URL versioning (v1, v2)',
    documentation: 'OpenAPI 3.0',
    errorFormat: {
      standard: {
        error: {
          code: 'string',
          message: 'string',
          details: 'object',
          timestamp: 'ISO8601',
          requestId: 'uuid',
        },
      },
    },
    rateLimiting: {
      default: '100 requests/minute',
      burst: '150 requests/minute',
    },
  },

  // Padrões de Segurança
  security: {
    authentication: 'JWT with RSA256',
    authorization: 'RBAC with fine-grained permissions',
    encryption: {
      atRest: 'AES-256-GCM',
      inTransit: 'TLS 1.3',
      secrets: 'Hashicorp Vault or equivalent',
    },
    headers: {
      required: [
        'Content-Security-Policy',
        'X-Frame-Options',
        'X-Content-Type-Options',
        'Strict-Transport-Security',
      ],
    },
  },

  // Padrões de Monitoramento
  monitoring: {
    metrics: {
      collection: 'Prometheus',
      visualization: 'Grafana',
      alerting: 'AlertManager',
    },
    logging: {
      format: 'JSON structured logs',
      levels: ['error', 'warn', 'info', 'debug', 'trace'],
      retention: '30 days',
      aggregation: 'ELK Stack',
    },
    tracing: {
      distributed: 'OpenTelemetry',
      sampling: '10%',
    },
  },

  // Padrões de Deploy
  deployment: {
    containers: 'Docker',
    orchestration: 'Kubernetes',
    registry: 'Private Docker Registry',
    ciCd: 'GitHub Actions',
    environments: {
      development: 'auto-deploy on push',
      staging: 'manual approval required',
      production: 'canary deployment with 10% traffic',
    },
  },
} as const;
```

## 4. Sistema de Monitoramento e Logs

```typescript
// src/core/monitoring/logger.ts
import winston from 'winston';
import { ElasticsearchTransport } from 'winston-elasticsearch';
import { MonitoringConfig } from '../../shared/config/monitoring';

export interface LogEntry {
  timestamp: string;
  level: 'error' | 'warn' | 'info' | 'debug' | 'trace';
  message: string;
  agent?: string;
  taskId?: string;
  userId?: string;
  duration?: number;
  error?: {
    name: string;
    message: string;
    stack?: string;
    code?: string;
  };
  metadata?: Record<string, any>;
}

export class StructuredLogger {
  private logger: winston.Logger;
  private static instance: StructuredLogger;

  private constructor() {
    const transports: winston.transport[] = [
      new winston.transports.Console({
        format: winston.format.combine(
          winston.format.timestamp(),
          winston.format.json()
        ),
      }),
      new winston.transports.File({
        filename: 'logs/error.log',
        level: 'error',
        maxsize: 5242880, // 5MB
        maxFiles: 5,
      }),
      new winston.transports.File({
        filename: 'logs/combined.log',
        maxsize: 5242880,
        maxFiles: 10,
      }),
    ];

    if (MonitoringConfig.elasticsearch.enabled) {
      transports.push(
        new ElasticsearchTransport({
          level: 'info',
          clientOpts: MonitoringConfig.elasticsearch,
          index: 'diyapp-logs',
        })
      );
    }

    this.logger = winston.createLogger({
      level: MonitoringConfig.logLevel,
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.timestamp(),
        winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
        winston.format.json()
      ),
      defaultMeta: {
        service: 'diyapp-v12',
        version: process.env.APP_VERSION || '1.0.0',
      },
      transports,
    });
  }

  public static getInstance(): StructuredLogger {
    if (!StructuredLogger.instance) {
      StructuredLogger.instance = new StructuredLogger();
    }
    return StructuredLogger.instance;
  }

  public log(entry: Omit<LogEntry, 'timestamp'>): void {
    const fullEntry: LogEntry = {
      ...entry,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    };

    this.logger.log({
      level: entry.level,
      message: entry.message,
      ...fullEntry,
    });
  }

  public error(error: Error, context?: Record<string, any>): void {
    this.log({
      level: 'error',
      message: error.message,
      error: {
        name: error.name,
        message: error.message,
        stack: error.stack,
      },
      metadata: context,
    });
  }

  public info(message: string, metadata?: Record<string, any>): void {
    this.log({
      level: 'info',
      message,
      metadata,
    });
  }

  public warn(message: string, metadata?: Record<string, any>): void {
    this.log({
      level: 'warn',
      message,
      metadata,
    });
  }

  public debug(message: string, metadata?: Record<string, any>): void {
    this.log({
      level: 'debug',
      message,
      metadata,
    });
  }

  public trace(message: string, metadata?: Record<string, any>): void {
    this.log({
      level: 'trace',
      message,
      metadata,
    });
  }

  public measure<T>(
    operation: string,
    fn: () => Promise<T>,
    metadata?: Record<string, any>
  ): Promise<T> {
    const startTime = Date.now();
    
    return fn()
      .then((result) => {
        const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
        this.info(`${operation} completed`, {
          ...metadata,
          duration,
          status: 'success',
        });
        return result;
      })
      .catch((error) => {
        const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
        this.error(error, {
          ...metadata,
          duration,
          status: 'failed',
          operation,
        });
        throw error;
      });
  }
}

// Métricas com Prometheus
import client from 'prom-client';

export class MetricsCollector {
  private static instance: MetricsCollector;
  private registry: client.Registry;

  // Métricas customizadas
  private agentRequests: client.Counter;
  private taskDuration: client.Histogram;
  private errorCounter: client.Counter;
  private queueSize: client.Gauge;
  private memoryUsage: client.Gauge;

  private constructor() {
    this.registry = new client.Registry();
    client.collectDefaultMetrics({ register: this.registry });

    // Inicializar métricas customizadas
    this.agentRequests = new client.Counter({
      name: 'diyapp_agent_requests_total',
      help: 'Total requests processed by agents',
      labelNames: ['agent', 'status'],
    });

    this.taskDuration = new client.Histogram({
      name: 'diyapp_task_duration_seconds',
      help: 'Duration of tasks in seconds',
      labelNames: ['task_type', 'agent'],
      buckets: [0.1, 0.5, 1, 2, 5, 10, 30],
    });

    this.errorCounter = new client.Counter({
      name: 'diyapp_errors_total',
      help: 'Total errors in the system',
      labelNames: ['type', 'agent', 'severity'],
    });

    this.queueSize = new client.Gauge({
      name: 'diyapp_queue_size',
      help: 'Current size of task queues',
      labelNames: ['queue_type'],
    });

    this.memoryUsage = new client.Gauge({
      name: 'diyapp_memory_usage_bytes',
      help: 'Memory usage in bytes',
      labelNames: ['type'],
    });

    // Registrar métricas
    this.registry.registerMetric(this.agentRequests);
    this.registry.registerMetric(this.taskDuration);
    this.registry.registerMetric(this.errorCounter);
    this.registry.registerMetric(this.queueSize);
    this.registry.registerMetric(this.memoryUsage);
  }

  public static getInstance(): MetricsCollector {
    if (!MetricsCollector.instance) {
      MetricsCollector.instance = new MetricsCollector();
    }
    return MetricsCollector.instance;
  }

  public recordAgentRequest(agent: string, status: 'success' | 'error'): void {
    this.agentRequests.inc({ agent, status });
  }

  public recordTaskDuration(
    taskType: string,
    agent: string,
    durationSeconds: number
  ): void {
    this.taskDuration.observe({ taskType, agent }, durationSeconds);
  }

  public recordError(
    type: string,
    agent: string,
    severity: 'low' | 'medium' | 'high' | 'critical'
  ): void {
    this.errorCounter.inc({ type, agent, severity });
  }

  public setQueueSize(queueType: string, size: number): void {
    this.queueSize.set({ queueType }, size);
  }

  public updateMemoryMetrics(): void {
    const memory = process.memoryUsage();
    this.memoryUsage.set({ type: 'rss' }, memory.rss);
    this.memoryUsage.set({ type: 'heapTotal' }, memory.heapTotal);
    this.memoryUsage.set({ type: 'heapUsed' }, memory.heapUsed);
    this.memoryUsage.set({ type: 'external' }, memory.external);
  }

  public async getMetrics(): Promise<string> {
    this.updateMemoryMetrics();
    return this.registry.metrics();
  }
}

// Health Check System
export class HealthChecker {
  private checks: Map<string, () => Promise<boolean>> = new Map();
  private logger = StructuredLogger.getInstance();

  public registerCheck(name: string, checkFn: () => Promise<boolean>): void {
    this.checks.set(name, checkFn);
  }

  public async checkAll(): Promise<{
    status: 'healthy' | 'unhealthy';
    checks: Record<string, boolean>;
    timestamp: string;
  }> {
    const results: Record<string, boolean> = {};
    const startTime = Date.now();

    for (const [name, checkFn] of this.checks) {
      try {
        const result = await checkFn();
        results[name] = result;
        
        if (!result) {
          this.logger.warn(`Health check failed: ${name}`);
        }
      } catch (error) {
        results[name] = false;
        this.logger.error(error as Error, { healthCheck: name });
      }
    }

    const allHealthy = Object.values(results).every((r) => r);
    const duration = Date.now() - startTime;

    this.logger.info('Health check completed', {
      status: allHealthy ? 'healthy' : 'unhealthy',
      duration,
      failedChecks: Object.entries(results)
        .filter(([_, r]) => !r)
        .map(([name]) => name),
    });

    return {
      status: allHealthy ? 'healthy' : 'unhealthy',
      checks: results,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    };
  }
}
```

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution V12 - Design System

Vou criar um Design System completo e premium para a V12, com foco em acessibilidade, componentes reutilizáveis e microinterações. O sistema será implementado como uma biblioteca CSS/JS modular.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-design-system-v12/
├── index.html              # Dashboard/Interface do Design System
├── package.json
├── README.md
├── src/
│   ├── design-system/
│   │   ├── tokens/         # Tokens de design
│   │   ├── components/     # Componentes UI
│   │   ├── utilities/      # Utilitários
│   │   └── animations/     # Microinterações
│   ├── docs/              # Documentação
│   └── examples/          # Exemplos de uso
└── public/
    └── assets/
        └── fonts/
```

# Backend APIs com Performance, Resiliência e Observabilidade

"""

# src/config.py
import os
from typing import Optional
from pydantic_settings import BaseSettings
from functools import lru_cache


class Settings(BaseSettings):
    # Application
    app_name: str = "DIYAPP Evolution V12"
    app_version: str = "v12.0.0"
    debug: bool = False
    environment: str = "production"
    
    # API
    api_prefix: str = "/api/v12"
    cors_origins: list = ["*"]
    
    # Database
    database_url: str = os.getenv("DATABASE_URL", "postgresql://user:pass@localhost:5432/diyapp")
    database_pool_size: int = 20
    database_max_overflow: int = 10
    
    # Redis (Cache)
    redis_url: str = os.getenv("REDIS_URL", "redis://localhost:6379/0")
    redis_cache_ttl: int = 300  # 5 minutes
    
    # External Services
    payment_service_url: str = os.getenv("PAYMENT_SERVICE_URL", "https://payments.example.com")
    notification_service_url: str = os.getenv("NOTIFICATION_SERVICE_URL", "https://notifications.example.com")
    
    # Timeouts (in seconds)
    database_timeout: int = 5
    external_service_timeout: int = 10
    llm_service_timeout: int = 30  # LLMs são mais lentos
    
    # Circuit Breaker
    circuit_breaker_failure_threshold: int = 5
    circuit_breaker_recovery_timeout: int = 60
    circuit_breaker_expected_exception: tuple = (Exception,)
    
    # Retry
    retry_max_attempts: int = 3
    retry_wait_multiplier: float = 1.5
    
    # Rate Limiting
    rate_limit_requests: int = 100
    rate_limit_window: int = 60  # seconds
    
    # Logging
    log_level: str = "INFO"
    log_format: str = "json"
    
    class Config:
        env_file = ".env"


@lru_cache()
def get_settings() -> Settings:
    return Settings()


# src/utils/circuit_breaker.py
import asyncio
from typing import Any, Callable, Optional
from circuitbreaker import circuit
from functools import wraps
import time


class CircuitBreaker:
    """Circuit breaker com fallback assíncrono"""
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        failure_threshold: int = 5,
        recovery_timeout: int = 60,
        expected_exception: tuple = (Exception,),
        name: str = "default"
    ):
        self.failure_threshold = failure_threshold
        self.recovery_timeout = recovery_timeout
        self.expected_exception = expected_exception
        self.name = name
        
    def __call__(self, fallback: Optional[Callable] = None):
        def decorator(func):
            @wraps(func)
            async def async_wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
                try:
                    # Usa circuit breaker síncrono com wrapper assíncrono
                    @circuit(
                        failure_threshold=self.failure_threshold,
                        recovery_timeout=self.recovery_timeout,
                        expected_exception=self.expected_exception,
                        name=self.name
                    )
                    def sync_wrapper():
                        # Para funções assíncronas, rodamos em event loop
                        return asyncio.run(func(*args, **kwargs))
                    
                    return await func(*args, **kwargs)
                except Exception as e:
                    if fallback:
                        return await fallback(*args, **kwargs)
                    raise
                    
            @wraps(func)
            def sync_wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
                try:
                    @circuit(
                        failure_threshold=self.failure_threshold,
                        recovery_timeout=self.recovery_timeout,
                        expected_exception=self.expected_exception,
                        name=self.name
                    )
                    def protected_func():
                        return func(*args, **kwargs)
                    
                    return protected_func()
                except Exception as e:
                    if fallback:
                        return fallback(*args, **kwargs)
                    raise
                    
            return async_wrapper if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(func) else sync_wrapper
        return decorator


# src/utils/retry.py
from tenacity import (
    retry,
    stop_after_attempt,
    wait_exponential,
    retry_if_exception_type,
    before_sleep_log
)
import logging
from typing import Type, Tuple


def create_retry_decorator(
    max_attempts: int = 3,
    wait_multiplier: float = 1.0,
    retry_exceptions: Tuple[Type[Exception], ...] = (Exception,),
    logger_name: str = "retry"
):
    """Cria decorator de retry com backoff exponencial"""
    
    logger = logging.getLogger(logger_name)
    
    return retry(
        stop=stop_after_attempt(max_attempts),
        wait=wait_exponential(multiplier=wait_multiplier, min=1, max=10),
        retry=retry_if_exception_type(retry_exceptions),
        before_sleep=before_sleep_log(logger, logging.WARNING),
        reraise=True
    )


# src/utils/cache.py
import redis.asyncio as redis
import pickle
from typing import Any, Optional
import hashlib
import json
from src.config import get_settings


class RedisCache:
    """Cache distribuído com Redis"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.settings = get_settings()
        self.redis_client: Optional[redis.Redis] = None
        
    async def connect(self):
        """Conecta ao Redis"""
        if not self.redis_client:
            self.redis_client = redis.from_url(
                self.settings.redis_url,
                encoding="utf-8",
                decode_responses=False
            )
    
    async def disconnect(self):
        """Desconecta do Redis"""
        if self.redis_client:
            await self.redis_client.close()
    
    def _generate_key(self, prefix: str, *args, **kwargs) -> str:
        """Gera chave de cache única"""
        key_data = f"{prefix}:{str(args)}:{json.dumps(kwargs, sort_keys=True)}"
        return f"cache:{hashlib.md5(key_data.encode()).hexdigest()}"
    
    async def get(self, key: str) -> Any:
        """Obtém valor do cache"""
        if not self.redis_client:
            await self.connect()
        
        try:
            data = await self.redis_client.get(key)
            if data:
                return pickle.loads(data)
        except Exception:
            # Se cache falhar, retorna None (degraça)
            return None
    
    async def set(self, key: str, value: Any, ttl: Optional[int] = None) -> bool:
        """Define valor no cache"""
        if not self.redis_client:
            await self.connect()
        
        try:
            ttl = ttl or self.settings.redis_cache_ttl
            serialized = pickle.dumps(value)
            return await self.redis_client.setex(key, ttl, serialized)
        except Exception:
            # Se cache falhar, apenas loga e continua
            return False
    
    async def delete(self, key: str) -> bool:
        """Remove valor do cache"""
        if not self.redis_client:
            await self.connect()
        
        try:
            return await self.redis_client.delete(key) > 0
        except Exception:
            return False
    
    async def clear_pattern(self, pattern: str) -> int:
        """Limpa cache por padrão"""
        if not self.redis_client:
            await self.connect()
        
        try:
            keys = await self.redis_client.keys(pattern)
            if keys:
                return await self.redis_client.delete(*keys)
            return 0
        except Exception:
            return 0


# Decorator de cache
def cached(ttl: Optional[int] = None, prefix: str = "default"):
    """Decorator para cache automático de resultados de função"""
    def decorator(func):
        @wraps(func)
        async def async_wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
            cache = RedisCache()
            cache_key = cache._generate_key(f"{prefix}:{func.__name__}", *args, **kwargs)
            
            # Tenta obter do cache
            cached_result = await cache.get(cache_key)
            if cached_result is not None:
                return cached_result
            
            # Executa função e cacheia resultado
            result = await func(*args, **kwargs)
            await cache.set(cache_key, result, ttl)
            return result
        
        @wraps(func)
        def sync_wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
            # Para funções síncronas, não cacheamos por padrão
            # (poderia ser implementado com threading se necessário)
            return func(*args, **kwargs)
        
        return async_wrapper if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(func) else sync_wrapper
    return decorator


# src/utils/logging.py
import structlog
import logging
import sys
import time
from typing import Any, Dict
import uuid
from contextvars import ContextVar
import json


# Context var para correlation ID
correlation_id_var: ContextVar[str] = ContextVar("correlation_id", default="")


class StructuredLogger:
    """Logger estruturado em JSON"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = structlog.get_logger()
        
    def setup_logging(self, log_level: str = "INFO", log_format: str = "json"):
        """Configura logging estruturado"""
        
        # Remove handlers existentes
        for handler in logging.root.handlers[:]:
            logging.root.removeHandler(handler)
        
        # Configura structlog
        timestamper = structlog.processors.TimeStamper(fmt="iso")
        
        shared_processors = [
            structlog.contextvars.merge_contextvars,
            structlog.stdlib.add_logger_name,
            structlog.stdlib.add_log_level,
            timestamper,
            structlog.processors.StackInfoRenderer(),
        ]
        
        if log_format == "json":
            processors = shared_processors + [
                structlog.processors.format_exc_info,
                structlog.processors.JSONRenderer()
            ]
        else:
            processors = shared_processors + [
                structlog.processors.format_exc_info,
                structlog.dev.ConsoleRenderer()
            ]
        
        structlog.configure(
            processors=processors,
            wrapper_class=structlog.stdlib.AsyncBoundLogger,
            logger_factory=structlog.stdlib.LoggerFactory(),
            cache_logger_on_first_use=True,
        )
        
        # Configura logging padrão
        handler = logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout)
        handler.setFormatter(logging.Formatter("%(message)s"))
        
        root_logger = logging.getLogger()
        root_logger.addHandler(handler)
        root_logger.setLevel(getattr(logging, log_level.upper()))
    
    def bind(self, **kwargs):
        """Adiciona contexto ao logger"""
        return self.logger.bind(**kwargs)
    
    def info(self, event: str, **kwargs):
        """Log nível info"""
        self.logger.info(event, **kwargs)
    
    def warning(self, event: str, **kwargs):
        """Log nível warning"""
        self.logger.warning(event, **kwargs)
    
    def error(self, event: str, **kwargs):
        """Log nível error"""
        self.logger.error(event, **kwargs)
    
    def critical(self, event: str, **kwargs):
        """Log nível critical"""
        self.logger.critical(event, **kwargs)
    
    def mask_sensitive_data(self, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Mascara dados sensíveis para logs"""
        masked = data.copy()
        sensitive_fields = ["password", "token", "api_key", "secret", "credit_card", "cpf", "email"]
        
        for field in sensitive_fields:
            if field in masked:
                if isinstance(masked[field], str) and len(masked[field]) > 4:
                    masked[field] = masked[field][:2] + "***" + masked[field][-2:]
                else:
                    masked[field] = "***"
        
        return masked


# Middleware para correlation ID
async def correlation_id_middleware(request, call_next):
    """Middleware para adicionar correlation ID a cada request"""
    correlation_id = request.headers.get("X-Correlation-ID", str(uuid.uuid4()))
    correlation_id_var.set(correlation_id)
    
    response = await call_next(request)
    response.headers["X-Correlation-ID"] = correlation_id
    
    return response


# src/health/checks.py
from typing import Dict, Any
import asyncio
import asyncpg
import redis.asyncio as redis
import httpx
from src.config import get_settings


class HealthChecker:
    """Sistema de health checks"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.settings = get_settings()
    
    async def check_database(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Verifica saúde do banco de dados"""
        try:
            conn = await asyncpg.connect(self.settings.database_url)
            await conn.execute("SELECT 1")
            await conn.close()
            return {"status": "healthy", "latency": 0}
        except Exception as e:
            return {"status": "unhealthy", "error": str(e)}
    
    async def check_redis(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Verifica saúde do Redis"""
        try:
            start = time.time()
            client = redis.from_url(self.settings.redis_url)
            await client.ping()
            latency = time.time() - start
            await client.close()
            return {"status": "healthy", "latency": latency}
        except Exception as e:
            return {"status": "unhealthy", "error": str(e)}
    
    async def check_payment_service(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Verifica saúde do serviço de pagamento"""
        try:
            async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=5.0) as client:
                start = time.time()
                response = await client.get(f"{self.settings.payment_service_url}/health")
                latency = time.time() - start
                
                if response.status_code == 200:
                    return {"status": "healthy", "latency": latency}
                else:
                    return {"status": "unhealthy", "status_code": response.status_code}
        except Exception as e:
            return {"status": "unhealthy", "error": str(e)}
    
    async def check_all(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Executa todos os health checks"""
        checks = {
            "database": self.check_database(),
            "redis": self.check_redis(),
            "payment_service": self.check_payment_service(),
        }
        
        results = {}
        for name, check in checks.items():
            results[name] = await check
        
        # Determina status geral
        all_healthy = all(r["status"] == "healthy" for r in results.values())
        overall_status = "healthy" if all_healthy else "degraded"
        
        return {
            "status": overall_status,
            "timestamp": time.time(),
            "version": self.settings.app_version,
            "checks": results
        }


# src/metrics/metrics.py
from prometheus_client import Counter, Histogram, Gauge, generate_latest, REGISTRY
import time
from typing import Callable
from fastapi import Request, Response


# Métricas
REQUEST_COUNT = Counter(
    "http_requests_total",
    "Total HTTP requests",
    ["method", "endpoint", "status"]
)

REQUEST_LATENCY = Histogram(
    "http_request_duration_seconds",
    "HTTP request latency",
    ["method", "endpoint"],
    buckets=[0.01, 0.05, 0.1, 0.3, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0, 5.0]
)

ACTIVE_REQUESTS = Gauge(
    "http_requests_active",
    "Active HTTP requests"
)

DATABASE_QUERIES = Counter(
    "database_queries_total",
    "Total database queries",
    ["operation", "table"]
)

EXTERNAL_CALLS = Counter(
    "external_calls_total",
    "Total external service calls",
    ["service", "status"]
)

CACHE_HITS = Counter(
    "cache_hits_total",
    "Total cache hits",
    ["type"]
)

CACHE_MISSES = Counter(
    "cache_misses_total",
    "Total cache misses",
    ["type"]
)


class MetricsMiddleware:
    """Middleware para coletar métricas"""
    
    def __init__(self, app):
        self.app = app
    
    async def __call__(self, scope, receive, send):
        if scope["type"] != "http":
            return await self.app(scope, receive, send)
        
        request = Request(scope, receive)
        method =

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
```typescript
// ============================================
// DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core
// Sistema de Design + Otimizações de Performance
// ============================================

// ADR: React 18 + TypeScript + Vite + Tailwind CSS
// Design System Token-Based com otimizações de bundle

// ESTRUTURA DO PROJETO:
// src/
//   ├── design-system/          # Sistema de Design
//   │   ├── tokens/            # Tokens de design
//   │   ├── components/        # Componentes base
//   │   └── hooks/             # Hooks do design system
//   ├── core/                  # Núcleo da aplicação
//   │   ├── state/            # Gerenciamento de estado
//   │   ├── utils/            # Utilitários
//   │   └── constants/        # Constantes
//   ├── features/              # Features com code splitting
//   │   ├── dashboard/        # Dashboard (lazy)
//   │   ├── editor/           # Editor (lazy)
//   │   └── analytics/        # Analytics (lazy)
//   ├── App.tsx               # Componente raiz
//   └── main.tsx              # Ponto de entrada
// public/
//   ├── index.html            # Dashboard principal
//   └── assets/               # Assets otimizados
// ============================================

// 1. TOKENS DO DESIGN SYSTEM
// src/design-system/tokens/index.ts
export const designTokens = {
  // Cores (sistema token-based)
  colors: {
    primary: {
      50: '#eff6ff',
      100: '#dbeafe',
      200: '#bfdbfe',
      300: '#93c5fd',
      400: '#60a5fa',
      500: '#3b82f6', // Primary

      700: '#1d4ed8',

      900: '#1e3a8a',

      success: '#10b981',

  typography: {
    fontFamily: {

      mono: ['JetBrains Mono', 'monospace'],

    fontSize: {
      xs: '0.75rem',    // 12px
      sm: '0.875rem',   // 14px
      base: '1rem',     // 16px
      lg: '1.125rem',   // 18px

      '2xl': '1.5rem',  // 24px
      '3xl': '1.875rem', // 30px
      '4xl': '2.25rem',  // 36px
    },
    fontWeight: {
      normal: '400',
      medium: '500',
      semibold: '600',
      bold: '700',
    },
    lineHeight: {
      tight: '1.25',
      normal: '1.5',
      relaxed: '1.75',
    },
  },
  
  // Espaçamento (sistema 8px base)
  spacing: {
    0: '0',
    1: '0.25rem',   // 4px
    2: '0.5rem',    // 8px
    3: '0.75rem',   // 12px
    4: '1rem',      // 16px
    5: '1.25rem',   // 20px

    8: '2rem',      // 32px
    10: '2.5rem',   // 40px
    12: '3rem',     // 48px
    16: '4rem',     // 64px
  },
  
  // Breakpoints responsivos
  breakpoints: {
    sm: '640px',
    md: '768px',
    lg: '1024px',
    xl: '1280px',
    '2xl': '1536px',
  },
  
  // Bordas e sombras
  borders: {
    radius: {
      none: '0',
      sm: '0.125rem',   // 2px
      md: '0.375rem',   // 6px
      lg: '0.5rem',     // 8px
      full: '9999px',
    },
    width: {
      thin: '1px',
      medium: '2px',
      thick: '4px',
    },
  },
  
  shadows: {
    sm: '0 1px 2px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.05)',
    md: '0 4px 6px -1px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
    lg: '0 10px 15px -3px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
    xl: '0 20px 25px -5px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',

  zIndex: {
    hide: -1,
    base: 0,
    docked: 10,
    dropdown: 1000,
    sticky: 1100,
    banner: 1200,
    overlay: 1300,
    modal: 1400,
    popover: 1500,
    toast: 1600,
    tooltip: 1700,
  },
} as const;

// Tipo para os tokens
export type DesignTokens = typeof designTokens;
export type ColorToken = keyof typeof designTokens.colors.primary;

// 2. PROVIDER DO DESIGN SYSTEM
// src/design-system/DesignSystemProvider.tsx
import React, { createContext, useContext, ReactNode } from 'react';
import { designTokens, DesignTokens } from './tokens';

const DesignSystemContext = createContext<DesignTokens>(designTokens);

interface DesignSystemProviderProps {
  children: ReactNode;
  tokens?: Partial<DesignTokens>;
}

export const DesignSystemProvider: React.FC<DesignSystemProviderProps> = ({
  children,
  tokens = {},
}) => {
  const mergedTokens = {
    ...designTokens,
    ...tokens,
  };

  return (
    <DesignSystemContext.Provider value={mergedTokens}>
      {children}
    </DesignSystemContext.Provider>
  );
};

export const useDesignTokens = () => {
  const context = useContext(DesignSystemContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error('useDesignTokens must be used within DesignSystemProvider');
  }
  return context;
};

// 3. COMPONENTE BASE COM ACESSIBILIDADE
// src/design-system/components/BaseButton.tsx
import React, { ButtonHTMLAttributes, forwardRef } from 'react';
import { useDesignTokens } from '../DesignSystemProvider';

interface BaseButtonProps extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'ghost' | 'danger';
  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
  isLoading?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  fullWidth?: boolean;
}

export const BaseButton = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, BaseButtonProps>(
  (
    {
      children,
      variant = 'primary',
      size = 'md',
      isLoading = false,
      leftIcon,
      rightIcon,
      fullWidth = false,
      disabled,
      className = '',
      ...props
    },
    ref
  ) => {
    const tokens = useDesignTokens();
    
    // Mapeamento de variantes para classes CSS
    const variantClasses = {
      primary: `bg-${tokens.colors.primary[500]} text-white hover:bg-${tokens.colors.primary[600]} focus:ring-2 focus:ring-${tokens.colors.primary[500]} focus:ring-offset-2`,
      secondary: `bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[200]} text-${tokens.colors.neutral[800]} hover:bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[300]} focus:ring-2 focus:ring-${tokens.colors.neutral[500]}`,
      ghost: `text-${tokens.colors.neutral[700]} hover:bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[100]} hover:text-${tokens.colors.neutral[900]}`,
      danger: `bg-${tokens.colors.semantic.error} text-white hover:bg-red-600 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-red-500`,
    };

    const sizeClasses = {
      sm: `px-${tokens.spacing[2]} py-${tokens.spacing[1]} text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.sm}`,
      md: `px-${tokens.spacing[4]} py-${tokens.spacing[2]} text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.base}`,
      lg: `px-${tokens.spacing[6]} py-${tokens.spacing[3]} text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.lg}`,
    };

    const baseClasses = `
      inline-flex items-center justify-center
      font-${tokens.typography.fontWeight.medium}
      rounded-${tokens.borders.radius.md}
      border border-transparent
      transition-all duration-${tokens.transitions.duration.fast}
      focus:outline-none focus:ring-2
      disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed
      ${fullWidth ? 'w-full' : ''}
      ${variantClasses[variant]}
      ${sizeClasses[size]}
      ${className}
    `.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();

    return (
      <button
        ref={ref}
        className={baseClasses}
        disabled={disabled || isLoading}
        aria-busy={isLoading}
        aria-disabled={disabled || isLoading}
        {...props}
      >
        {isLoading && (
          <svg
            className="animate-spin -ml-1 mr-2 h-4 w-4 text-current"
            xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
            fill="none"
            viewBox="0 0 24 24"
            aria-hidden="true"
          >
            <circle
              className="opacity-25"
              cx="12"
              cy="12"
              r="10"
              stroke="currentColor"
              strokeWidth="4"
            />
            <path
              className="opacity-75"
              fill="currentColor"
              d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"
            />
          </svg>
        )}
        {!isLoading && leftIcon && <span className="mr-2">{leftIcon}</span>}
        <span>{children}</span>
        {!isLoading && rightIcon && <span className="ml-2">{rightIcon}</span>}
      </button>
    );
  }
);

BaseButton.displayName = 'BaseButton';

// 4. GESTÃO DE ESTADO GLOBAL OTIMIZADO
// src/core/state/store.ts
import { createContext, useContext, useReducer, ReactNode, useCallback } from 'react';

// Tipos do estado
interface AppState {
  user: {
    id: string | null;
    name: string | null;
    email: string | null;
    preferences: {
      theme: 'light' | 'dark' | 'system';
      language: string;
      notifications: boolean;
    };
  };
  ui: {
    sidebarOpen: boolean;
    currentView: string;
    modals: Record<string, boolean>;
    notifications: Array<{
      id: string;
      type: 'info' | 'success' | 'warning' | 'error';
      message: string;
      timestamp: number;
    }>;
  };
  data: {
    projects: Record<string, any>;
    isLoading: boolean;
    lastUpdated: number | null;
  };
}

// Ações
type Action =
  | { type: 'SET_USER'; payload: Partial<AppState['user']> }
  | { type: 'TOGGLE_SIDEBAR' }
  | { type: 'SET_VIEW'; payload: string }
  | { type: 'SHOW_MODAL'; payload: string }
  | { type: 'HIDE_MODAL'; payload: string }
  | { type: 'ADD_NOTIFICATION'; payload: Omit<AppState['ui']['notifications'][0], 'id' | 'timestamp'> }
  | { type: 'REMOVE_NOTIFICATION'; payload: string }
  | { type: 'SET_PROJECTS'; payload: Record<string, any> }
  | { type: 'SET_LOADING'; payload: boolean };

// Estado inicial
const initialState: AppState = {
  user: {
    id: null,
    name: null,
    email: null,
    preferences: {
      theme: 'system',
      language: 'en',
      notifications: true,
    },
  },
  ui: {
    sidebarOpen: true,
    currentView: 'dashboard',
    modals: {},
    notifications: [],
  },
  data: {
    projects: {},
    isLoading: false,
    lastUpdated: null,
  },
};

// Reducer otimizado com Immer-like patterns
function appReducer(state: AppState, action: Action): AppState {
  switch (action.type) {
    case 'SET_USER':
      return {
        ...state,
        user: {
          ...state.user,
          ...action.payload,
          preferences: {
            ...state.user.preferences,
            ...(action.payload.preferences || {}),
          },
        },
      };

    case 'TOGGLE_SIDEBAR':
      return {
        ...state,
        ui: {
          ...state.ui,
          sidebarOpen: !state.ui.sidebarOpen,
        },
      };

    case 'SET_VIEW':
      return {
        ...state,
        ui: {
          ...state.ui,
          currentView: action.payload,
        },
      };

    case 'SHOW_MODAL':
      return {
        ...state,
        ui: {
          ...state.ui,
          modals: {
            ...state.ui.modals,
            [action.payload]: true,
          },
        },
      };

    case 'HIDE_MODAL':
      const newModals = { ...state.ui.modals };
      delete newModals[action.payload];
      return {
        ...state,
        ui: {
          ...state.ui,
          modals: newModals,
        },
      };

    case 'ADD_NOTIFICATION':
      const newNotification = {
        ...action.payload,
        id: Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9),
        timestamp: Date.now(),
      };
      return {
        ...state,
        ui: {
          ...state.ui,
          notifications: [...state.ui.notifications, newNotification].slice(-5), // Mantém apenas as 5 mais recentes
        },
      };

    case 'REMOVE_NOTIFICATION':
      return {
        ...state,
        ui: {
          ...state.ui,
          notifications: state.ui.notifications.filter(
            (n) => n.id !== action.payload
          ),
        },
      };

    case 'SET_PROJECTS':
      return {
        ...state,
        data: {
          ...state.data,
          projects: action.payload,
          lastUpdated: Date.now(),
        },
      };

    case 'SET_LOADING':
      return {
        ...state,
        data: {
          ...state.data,
          isLoading: action.payload,
        },
      };

    default:
      return state;
  }
}

// Contexto do estado
const AppStateContext = createContext<AppState | undefined>(undefined);
const AppDispatchContext = createContext<React.Dispatch<Action> | undefined>(undefined);

// Provider otimizado
interface AppStateProviderProps {
  children: ReactNode;
}

export const AppStateProvider: React.FC<AppStateProviderProps> = ({ children }) => {
  const [state, dispatch] = useReducer(appReducer, initialState);

  // Memoização do provider value
  const stateValue = state;
  const dispatchValue = dispatch;

  return (
    <AppStateContext.Provider value={stateValue}>
      <AppDispatchContext.Provider value={dispatchValue}>
        {children}
      </AppDispatchContext.Provider>
    </AppStateContext.Provider>
  );
};

// Hooks otimizados
export const useAppState = () => {
  const context = useContext(AppStateContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error('useAppState must be used within AppStateProvider');
  }
  return context;
};

export const useAppDispatch = () => {
  const context = useContext(AppDispatchContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error('useAppDispatch must be used within AppStateProvider');
  }
  return context;
};

// Hook específico para projetos (evita re-renders desnecessários)
export const useProjects = () => {
  const state = useAppState();
  return {
    projects: state.data.projects,
    isLoading: state.data.isLoading,
    lastUpdated: state.data

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
```dockerfile
# Dockerfile para aplicação principal
FROM node:18-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

# Instala dependências de build
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copia código da aplicação
COPY . .

# Cria usuário não-root para segurança
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs && \
    adduser -S nodejs -u 1001

USER nodejs

# Aplicação principal expõe na porta 3000
EXPOSE 3000

# Health check a cada 30s (conforme SLOs)
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=10s --retries=3 \
    CMD wget --no-verbose --tries=1 --spider http://localhost:3000/health || exit 1

CMD ["node", "src/server.js"]
```

```dockerfile
# Dockerfile para serviço de monitoramento
FROM python:3.11-slim AS monitor

WORKDIR /monitor

# Instala dependências de monitoramento
COPY requirements-monitor.txt .
RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements-monitor.txt

# Copia scripts de monitoramento
COPY monitor/ .

# Cria usuário não-root
RUN useradd -m -u 1002 monitor
USER monitor

CMD ["python", "monitor/main.py"]
```

```yaml
# docker-compose.yml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Aplicação principal
  app:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    container_name: diyapp-main
    restart: unless-stopped  # Restart automático exceto se parado manualmente
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - LOG_LEVEL=info
      - PORT=3000
    volumes:
      - app-logs:/app/logs
      - ./config:/app/config:ro
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    depends_on:
      - postgres
      - redis
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "wget", "--no-verbose", "--tries=1", "--spider", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 3s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 10s

  # Banco de dados PostgreSQL
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-postgres
    restart: always  # Sempre reinicia - crítico para dados
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_USER=diyapp
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${DB_PASSWORD}
      - POSTGRES_DB=diyapp_prod
    volumes:
      - postgres-data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./init-db:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d:ro
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Cache Redis
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    restart: always
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes --requirepass ${REDIS_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - redis-data:/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "--raw", "incr", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 3s
      retries: 3

  # Serviço de monitoramento
  monitor:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.monitor
    container_name: diyapp-monitor
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      - PROMETHEUS_URL=http://prometheus:9090
      - GRAFANA_URL=http://grafana:3000
      - APP_URL=http://app:3000
    volumes:
      - ./monitor/config:/monitor/config:ro
      - monitor-data:/monitor/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    depends_on:
      - prometheus
      - grafana

  # Prometheus para métricas
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:v2.45.0
    container_name: diyapp-prometheus
    restart: unless-stopped
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
      - '--web.console.libraries=/etc/prometheus/console_libraries'
      - '--web.console.templates=/etc/prometheus/consoles'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=30d'
      - '--web.enable-lifecycle'
    volumes:
      - prometheus-data:/prometheus
      - ./monitoring/prometheus:/etc/prometheus:ro
      - ./monitoring/alerts:/etc/prometheus/alerts:ro
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Grafana para dashboards
  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:10.0.0
    container_name: diyapp-grafana
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=${GRAFANA_PASSWORD}
      - GF_INSTALL_PLUGINS=grafana-piechart-panel
    volumes:
      - grafana-data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./monitoring/grafana/provisioning:/etc/grafana/provisioning:ro
      - ./monitoring/grafana/dashboards:/etc/grafana/dashboards:ro
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    depends_on:
      - prometheus

  # Node Exporter para métricas do host
  node-exporter:
    image: prom/node-exporter:v1.6.0
    container_name: diyapp-node-exporter
    restart: unless-stopped
    command:
      - '--path.rootfs=/host'
    pid: host
    volumes:
      - /:/host:ro,rslave
    ports:
      - "9100:9100"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # cAdvisor para métricas de containers
  cadvisor:
    image: gcr.io/cadvisor/cadvisor:v0.47.2
    container_name: diyapp-cadvisor
    restart: unless-stopped
    volumes:
      - /:/rootfs:ro
      - /var/run:/var/run:ro
      - /sys:/sys:ro
      - /var/lib/docker/:/var/lib/docker:ro
      - /dev/disk/:/dev/disk:ro
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Alertmanager para notificações
  alertmanager:
    image: prom/alertmanager:v0.25.0
    container_name: diyapp-alertmanager
    restart: unless-stopped
    volumes:
      - alertmanager-data:/alertmanager
      - ./monitoring/alertmanager:/etc/alertmanager:ro
    ports:
      - "9093:9093"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/alertmanager/config.yml'
      - '--storage.path=/alertmanager'

networks:
  diyapp-network:
    driver: bridge
    name: diyapp-network

volumes:
  postgres-data:
    name: diyapp-postgres-data
  redis-data:
    name: diyapp-redis-data
  app-logs:
    name: diyapp-app-logs
  prometheus-data:
    name: diyapp-prometheus-data
  grafana-data:
    name: diyapp-grafana-data
  alertmanager-data:
    name: diyapp-alertmanager-data
  monitor-data:
    name: diyapp-monitor-data
```

```yaml
# monitoring/prometheus/prometheus.yml
global:
  scrape_interval: 15s
  evaluation_interval: 15s

rule_files:
  - "alerts/*.yml"

scrape_configs:
  - job_name: 'prometheus'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['localhost:9090']

  - job_name: 'app'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['app:3000']
    metrics_path: '/metrics'
    scrape_interval: 30s

  - job_name: 'node'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['node-exporter:9100']

  - job_name: 'cadvisor'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['cadvisor:8080']
    scrape_interval: 15s

  - job_name: 'postgres'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['postgres:9187']

  - job_name: 'redis'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['redis:9121']

alerting:
  alertmanagers:
    - static_configs:
        - targets: ['alertmanager:9093']
```

```yaml
# monitoring/prometheus/alerts/slos.yml
groups:
  - name: slos
    rules:
      # SLO: Disponibilidade 99.9% (43.8 min downtime/mês)
      - alert: AvailabilitySLOBreach
        expr: |
          sum(rate(http_requests_total{job="app", code!~"5.."}[5m])) 
          / sum(rate(http_requests_total{job="app"}[5m])) * 100 < 99.9
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: sev2
          slo: availability
        annotations:
          summary: "Disponibilidade abaixo do SLO de 99.9%"
          description: "Disponibilidade atual: {{ $value }}%. Error budget sendo consumido rapidamente."
          runbook_url: "https://github.com/diyapp/runbooks/blob/main/availability.md"

      # SLO: Error rate < 0.1%
      - alert: ErrorRateSLOBreach
        expr: |
          sum(rate(http_requests_total{job="app", code=~"5.."}[1h])) 
          / sum(rate(http_requests_total{job="app"}[1h])) * 100 > 0.1
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: sev2
          slo: error_rate
        annotations:
          summary: "Error rate acima do SLO de 0.1%"
          description: "Error rate atual: {{ $value }}%. Investigação imediata necessária."
          runbook_url: "https://github.com/diyapp/runbooks/blob/main/error-rate.md"

      # SLO: Latência P95 API < 300ms
      - alert: LatencySLOBreach
        expr: |
          histogram_quantile(0.95, sum(rate(http_request_duration_seconds_bucket{job="app", endpoint!~".*llm.*"}[5m])) by (le)) > 0.3
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: sev2
          slo: latency
        annotations:
          summary: "Latência P95 acima de 300ms"
          description: "Latência P95 atual: {{ $value }}s. Performance degradada."
          runbook_url: "https://github.com/diyapp/runbooks/blob/main/latency.md"

      # SLO: Latência LLM P95 < 8s
      - alert: LLMLatencySLOBreach
        expr: |
          histogram_quantile(0.95, sum(rate(llm_request_duration_seconds_bucket{job="app"}[5m])) by (le, provider)) > 8
        for: 2m
        labels:
          severity: sev2
          slo: llm_latency
        annotations:
          summary: "Latência LLM P95 acima de 8s"
          description: "Latência LLM P95 para {{ $labels.provider }}: {{ $value }}s"
          runbook_url: "https://github.com/diyapp/runbooks/blob/main/llm-latency.md"

      # Error Budget Burn Rate Alerts
      - alert: ErrorBudgetBurnRateHigh
        expr: |
          (
            (1 - (sum(rate(http_requests_total{job="app", code!~"5.."}[1h])) / sum(rate(http_requests_total{job="app"}[1h]))))
            / (1 - 0.999)
          ) > 5
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: sev1
          slo: error_budget
        annotations:
          summary: "Error budget sendo consumido 5x mais rápido que o esperado"
          description: "Burn rate: {{ $value }}. Budget será esgotado em horas."
          runbook_url: "https://github.com/diyapp/runbooks/blob/main/error-budget.md"

      - alert: ErrorBudgetCritical
        expr: |
          (
            (1 - (sum(rate(http_requests_total{job="app", code!~"5.."}[7d])) / sum(rate(http_requests_total{job="app"}[7d]))))
            / (1 - 0.999) * 100
          ) > 80
        for: 0m
        labels:
          severity: sev1
          slo: error_budget
        annotations:
          summary: "Error budget crítico: 80% consumido"
          description: "{{ $value }}% do error budget consumido. Freeze de deploys recomendado."
          runbook_url: "https://github.com/diyapp/runbooks/blob/main/error-budget.md"
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
```sql
-- ============================================
-- DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core
-- Database Optimization Package
-- Data Engineer: Schema & Query Optimization
-- ============================================

-- ============================================
-- PARTE 1: ANÁLISE DE PERFORMANCE ATUAL
-- ============================================

-- Script de análise de performance (executar na V11 antes da migração)
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW v11_performance_analysis AS
SELECT 
    schemaname,
    tablename,
    pg_size_pretty(pg_total_relation_size(schemaname||'.'||tablename)) as total_size,
    pg_size_pretty(pg_relation_size(schemaname||'.'||tablename)) as table_size,
    pg_size_pretty(pg_total_relation_size(schemaname||'.'||tablename) - 
                   pg_relation_size(schemaname||'.'||tablename)) as index_size,
    n_live_tup as row_count,
    n_dead_tup as dead_rows,
    round((n_dead_tup::numeric / NULLIF(n_live_tup + n_dead_tup, 0)) * 100, 2) as dead_row_percentage
FROM pg_stat_user_tables 
JOIN pg_tables ON tablename = pg_tables.tablename
WHERE schemaname = 'public'
ORDER BY pg_total_relation_size(schemaname||'.'||tablename) DESC;

-- ============================================
-- PARTE 2: ESQUEMAS OTIMIZADOS V12
-- ============================================

-- 2.1 Schema principal otimizado com particionamento
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS v12_core;

-- Tabela de usuários com particionamento por tenant
CREATE TABLE v12_core.users (
    user_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    tenant_id UUID NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(320) NOT NULL,
    username VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    full_name VARCHAR(200),
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'active' CHECK (status IN ('active', 'inactive', 'suspended')),
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    deleted_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    CONSTRAINT unique_tenant_email UNIQUE (tenant_id, email)
) PARTITION BY HASH (tenant_id);

-- Partições para tenants (exemplo: 4 partições)
CREATE TABLE v12_core.users_p0 PARTITION OF v12_core.users
    FOR VALUES WITH (MODULUS 4, REMAINDER 0);

CREATE TABLE v12_core.users_p1 PARTITION OF v12_core.users
    FOR VALUES WITH (MODULUS 4, REMAINDER 1);

CREATE TABLE v12_core.users_p2 PARTITION OF v12_core.users
    FOR VALUES WITH (MODULUS 4, REMAINDER 2);

CREATE TABLE v12_core.users_p3 PARTITION OF v12_core.users
    FOR VALUES WITH (MODULUS 4, REMAINDER 3);

-- 2.2 Tabela de eventos com particionamento por tempo
CREATE TABLE v12_core.events (
    event_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL,
    event_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    event_data JSONB NOT NULL,
    session_id UUID,
    ip_address INET,
    user_agent TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
) PARTITION BY RANGE (created_at);

-- Partições mensais para eventos (auto-criar via script)
CREATE TABLE v12_core.events_2024_01 PARTITION OF v12_core.events
    FOR VALUES FROM ('2024-01-01') TO ('2024-02-01');

CREATE TABLE v12_core.events_2024_02 PARTITION OF v12_core.events
    FOR VALUES FROM ('2024-02-01') TO ('2024-03-01');

-- 2.3 Tabela de documentos com FULL TEXT SEARCH otimizado
CREATE TABLE v12_core.documents (
    document_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    tenant_id UUID NOT NULL,
    title VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
    content TEXT NOT NULL,
    content_tsvector TSVECTOR GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        to_tsvector('portuguese', coalesce(title, '') || ' ' || coalesce(content, ''))
    ) STORED,
    category VARCHAR(100),
    tags TEXT[] DEFAULT '{}',
    version INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
    created_by UUID NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    deleted_at TIMESTAMPTZ
);

-- ============================================
-- PARTE 3: ÍNDICES ESTRATÉGICOS
-- ============================================

-- 3.1 Índices para tabela users
CREATE INDEX idx_users_tenant_status ON v12_core.users(tenant_id, status) 
    WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;

CREATE INDEX idx_users_email_lower ON v12_core.users(LOWER(email));
CREATE INDEX idx_users_created_at ON v12_core.users(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_metadata_gin ON v12_core.users USING GIN (metadata);

-- 3.2 Índices para tabela events
CREATE INDEX idx_events_user_created ON v12_core.events(user_id, created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_events_type_created ON v12_core.events(event_type, created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_events_session ON v12_core.events(session_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_events_data_gin ON v12_core.events USING GIN (event_data);
CREATE INDEX idx_events_created_at_brin ON v12_core.events USING BRIN (created_at);

-- 3.3 Índices para tabela documents
CREATE INDEX idx_documents_tenant ON v12_core.documents(tenant_id) 
    WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;

CREATE INDEX idx_documents_created_by ON v12_core.documents(created_by);
CREATE INDEX idx_documents_category ON v12_core.documents(category);
CREATE INDEX idx_documents_tags_gin ON v12_core.documents USING GIN (tags);
CREATE INDEX idx_documents_content_fts ON v12_core.documents USING GIN (content_tsvector);
CREATE INDEX idx_documents_updated_at ON v12_core.documents(updated_at DESC);

-- ============================================
-- PARTE 4: SCRIPTS DE MIGRAÇÃO SEGURA
-- ============================================

-- 4.1 Script de migração incremental com validação
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION migrate_v11_to_v12()
RETURNS TABLE (
    table_name TEXT,
    rows_migrated BIGINT,
    migration_duration INTERVAL,
    validation_passed BOOLEAN
) AS $$
DECLARE
    start_time TIMESTAMPTZ;
    end_time TIMESTAMPTZ;
    row_count BIGINT;
    expected_count BIGINT;
BEGIN
    -- Migração de usuários com validação de consistência
    start_time := clock_timestamp();
    
    INSERT INTO v12_core.users (
        user_id, tenant_id, email, username, full_name, 
        status, metadata, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at
    )
    SELECT 
        u.id, u.tenant_id, u.email, u.username, u.full_name,
        COALESCE(u.status, 'active'), 
        jsonb_build_object(
            'phone', u.phone,
            'department', u.department,
            'custom_fields', u.custom_data
        ),
        u.created_at, u.updated_at, u.deleted_at
    FROM v11_legacy.users u
    WHERE u.deleted_at IS NULL
    ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING;
    
    GET DIAGNOSTICS row_count = ROW_COUNT;
    end_time := clock_timestamp();
    
    -- Validação
    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO expected_count 
    FROM v11_legacy.users 
    WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
    
    RETURN QUERY SELECT 
        'users'::TEXT,
        row_count,
        (end_time - start_time),
        (row_count = expected_count);
    
    -- Migração de documentos com transformação
    start_time := clock_timestamp();
    
    INSERT INTO v12_core.documents (
        document_id, tenant_id, title, content, category,
        tags, version, created_by, created_at, updated_at
    )
    SELECT 
        d.id, d.tenant_id, d.title, d.content, d.category,
        string_to_array(d.tags, ',')::TEXT[],
        d.version, d.created_by, d.created_at, d.updated_at
    FROM v11_legacy.documents d
    WHERE d.deleted_at IS NULL;
    
    GET DIAGNOSTICS row_count = ROW_COUNT;
    end_time := clock_timestamp();
    
    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO expected_count 
    FROM v11_legacy.documents 
    WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
    
    RETURN QUERY SELECT 
        'documents'::TEXT,
        row_count,
        (end_time - start_time),
        (row_count = expected_count);
    
    -- Migração de eventos em batches para evitar locks
    start_time := clock_timestamp();
    
    WITH event_batches AS (
        SELECT * FROM v11_legacy.events
        WHERE created_at >= '2024-01-01'
        ORDER BY created_at
        LIMIT 100000
    )
    INSERT INTO v12_core.events (
        event_id, user_id, event_type, event_data, 
        session_id, ip_address, user_agent, created_at
    )
    SELECT 
        e.id, e.user_id, e.event_type, e.event_data,
        e.session_id, e.ip_address::INET, e.user_agent, e.created_at
    FROM event_batches e;
    
    GET DIAGNOSTICS row_count = ROW_COUNT;
    end_time := clock_timestamp();
    
    RETURN QUERY SELECT 
        'events_batch_1'::TEXT,
        row_count,
        (end_time - start_time),
        (row_count > 0);
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

-- 4.2 Script de rollback seguro
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION rollback_v12_migration()
RETURNS VOID AS $$
BEGIN
    -- Desabilitar triggers e constraints temporariamente
    ALTER TABLE v12_core.users DISABLE TRIGGER ALL;
    ALTER TABLE v12_core.events DISABLE TRIGGER ALL;
    ALTER TABLE v12_core.documents DISABLE TRIGGER ALL;
    
    -- Registrar rollback
    INSERT INTO v12_core.migration_log (
        migration_version, action, rows_affected, executed_at
    )
    VALUES ('v12', 'rollback', 
           (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v12_core.users) +
           (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v12_core.events) +
           (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM v12_core.documents),
           NOW());
    
    -- Limpar dados da V12 (cuidado em produção!)
    TRUNCATE TABLE v12_core.users CASCADE;
    TRUNCATE TABLE v12_core.events CASCADE;
    TRUNCATE TABLE v12_core.documents CASCADE;
    
    -- Reabilitar triggers e constraints
    ALTER TABLE v12_core.users ENABLE TRIGGER ALL;
    ALTER TABLE v12_core.events ENABLE TRIGGER ALL;
    ALTER TABLE v12_core.documents ENABLE TRIGGER ALL;
    
    RAISE NOTICE 'Rollback da migração V12 concluído com sucesso';
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

-- ============================================
-- PARTE 5: CONFIGURAÇÃO REDIS PARA CACHE
-- ============================================

-- 5.1 Script de configuração Redis (Node.js)
-- File: src/cache/redis-config.js
const Redis = require('ioredis');

class RedisCache {
    constructor() {
        this.client = new Redis({
            host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
            port: process.env.REDIS_PORT || 6379,
            password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD,
            retryStrategy: (times) => {
                const delay = Math.min(times * 50, 2000);
                return delay;
            },
            maxRetriesPerRequest: 3,
            enableReadyCheck: true,
        });

        this.client.on('error', (err) => {
            console.error('Redis error:', err);
        });

        this.client.on('connect', () => {
            console.log('Redis connected successfully');
        });
    }

    // Cache de usuários por ID (TTL: 5 minutos)
    async cacheUser(userId, userData) {
        const key = `user:${userId}`;
        await this.client.setex(
            key,
            300, // 5 minutos
            JSON.stringify(userData)
        );
        return userData;
    }

    // Cache de documentos com tags
    async cacheDocument(documentId, documentData) {
        const key = `document:${documentId}`;
        const tags = documentData.tags || [];
        
        const pipeline = this.client.pipeline();
        pipeline.setex(key, 600, JSON.stringify(documentData)); // 10 minutos
        
        // Indexar por tags
        tags.forEach(tag => {
            pipeline.sadd(`tag:${tag}:documents`, documentId);
        });
        
        await pipeline.exec();
        return documentData;
    }

    // Cache de queries frequentes
    async cacheQuery(queryKey, params, result) {
        const cacheKey = `query:${queryKey}:${JSON.stringify(params)}`;
        await this.client.setex(
            cacheKey,
            60, // 1 minuto para queries dinâmicas
            JSON.stringify(result)
        );
        return result;
    }

    // Invalidar cache por padrão
    async invalidatePattern(pattern) {
        const keys = await this.client.keys(pattern);
        if (keys.length > 0) {
            await this.client.del(...keys);
        }
        return keys.length;
    }

    // Health check
    async healthCheck() {
        try {
            await this.client.ping();
            return { status: 'healthy', client: 'redis' };
        } catch (error) {
            return { status: 'unhealthy', error: error.message };
        }
    }
}

module.exports = new RedisCache();

-- 5.2 Middleware de cache para queries PostgreSQL
-- File: src/db/query-with-cache.js
const redis = require('../cache/redis-config');
const { performance } = require('perf_hooks');

async function queryWithCache(pool, query, params = [], options = {}) {
    const {
        cacheKey,
        ttl = 60,
        bypassCache = false,
        invalidateOnWrite = false
    } = options;

    // Se não usar cache ou bypass ativado, executa query direto
    if (!cacheKey || bypassCache) {
        return pool.query(query, params);
    }

    const redisKey = `sql:${cacheKey}:${JSON.stringify(params)}`;
    
    // Tentar obter do cache
    if (!invalidateOnWrite) {
        const cached = await redis.client.get(redisKey);
        if (cached) {
            console.log(`Cache hit for key: ${redisKey}`);
            return { rows: JSON.parse(cached), fromCache: true };
        }
    }

    // Cache miss ou invalidação, executa query
    const startTime = performance.now();
    const result = await pool.query(query, params);
    const endTime = performance.now();
    
    console.log(`Query executed in ${(endTime - startTime).toFixed(2)}ms`);
    
    // Cache o resultado se for válido
    if (result.rows.length > 0 && !invalidateOnWrite) {
        await redis.client.setex(
            redisKey,
            ttl,
            JSON.stringify(result.rows)
        );
        console.log(`Cached result for key: ${redisKey} (TTL: ${ttl}s)`);
    }
    
    return { ...result, fromCache: false, queryTime: endTime - startTime };
}

// Exemplos de uso com cache
const cachedQueries = {
    // Usuários ativos por tenant
    getActiveUsersByTenant: async (tenantId) => {
        return queryWithCache(pool, 
            `SELECT user_id, email, username, created_at 
             FROM v12_core.users 
             WHERE tenant_id = $1 AND status = 'active' 
             ORDER BY created_at DESC`,
            [tenantId],
            { cacheKey: `active_users_${tenantId}`, ttl: 300 }
        );
    },

    // Documentos por tag com paginação
    getDocumentsByTag: async (tag, page = 1, limit = 20) => {
        const offset = (page - 1) * limit;
        return queryWithCache(pool,
            `SELECT document_id, title, category, created_at 
             FROM v12_core.documents 
             WHERE $1 = ANY(tags) AND deleted_at IS NULL
             ORDER BY updated_at DESC 
             LIMIT $2 OFFSET $3`,
            [tag, limit, offset],
            { cacheKey: `docs_tag_${tag}_page_${page}`, ttl: 120 }
        );
    },

    // Métricas agregadas (cache mais longo)
    getDailyMetrics: async (date) => {
        return queryWithCache(pool,
            `SELECT 
                COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as active_users,
                COUNT(*) as total_events,
                COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) as unique_sessions
             FROM v12_core.events
             WHERE created_at::date = $1`,
            [date],
            { cacheKey: `metrics_${date}`, ttl: 3600 } // 1 hora
        );
    }
};

module.exports = { queryWithCache, cachedQueries };

-- PARTE 6: MONITORAMENTO E MANUTENÇÃO

CREATE TABLE v12_core.query_performance (
    query_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    query_hash VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL,
    query_text TEXT NOT NULL,
    avg_execution_time DECIMAL(10,4),
    total_exec

## 1. Roteiro de Testes de Performance (Carga)

### 1.1 Plano de Testes de Carga

```javascript
// tests/performance/load/load_test_plan.js
/**
 * Roteiro de Testes de Performance - DIYAPP V12
 * Objetivo: Garantir que o sistema suporte 10.000 usuários concorrentes
 * com tempo de resposta < 2s para 95% das requisições
 */

const LoadTestPlan = {
  // Configurações de Ambiente
  environment: {
    staging: {
      baseUrl: 'https://staging.diyapp.com',
      expectedUsers: 10000,
      rampUpTime: '30m',
      testDuration: '2h'
    },
    production: {
      baseUrl: 'https://app.diyapp.com',
      expectedUsers: 50000,
      rampUpTime: '1h',
      testDuration: '4h'
    }
  },

  // Cenários de Carga
  scenarios: [
    {
      name: 'Cenário 1 - Navegação Básica',
      weight: 30,
      steps: [
        'Acessar página inicial',
        'Login de usuário',
        'Navegar pelo dashboard',
        'Acessar lista de projetos',
        'Logout'
      ],
      targetResponseTime: '1.5s',
      errorThreshold: '1%'
    },

### 1.2 Script de Teste de Carga com k6

```javascript
// tests/performance/k6/load_test.js
import http from 'k6/http';
import { check, sleep, group } from 'k6';
import { Rate, Trend } from 'k6/metrics';
import { htmlReport } from "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/benc-uk/k6-reporter/main/dist/bundle.js";

// Métricas customizadas
const errorRate = new Rate('errors');
const responseTimeTrend = new Trend('response_time');

// Configuração
export const options = {
  stages: [
    { duration: '5m', target: 100 },  // Ramp up
    { duration: '30m', target: 1000 }, // Carga normal
    { duration: '5m', target: 0 },     // Ramp down
  ],
  thresholds: {
    'http_req_duration': ['p(95)<2000', 'p(99)<3000'],
    'errors': ['rate<0.01'],
    'checks': ['rate>0.99']
  },
  ext: {
    loadimpact: {
      projectID: 123456,
      name: 'DIYAPP Load Test'
    }
  }
};

// Dados de teste
const testUsers = JSON.parse(open('./test_users.json'));

// Headers comuns
const headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  'User-Agent': 'k6-load-test',
  'Authorization': 'Bearer ${token}'
};

// Funções de teste
function login(user) {
  const payload = JSON.stringify({
    email: user.email,
    password: user.password
  });
  
  const res = http.post(`${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/v1/auth/login`, payload, {
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }
  });
  
  const success = check(res, {
    'login status 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
    'login has token': (r) => r.json('token') !== undefined
  });
  
  errorRate.add(!success);
  responseTimeTrend.add(res.timings.duration);
  
  return success ? res.json('token') : null;
}

function createProject(token, projectData) {
  const res = http.post(
    `${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/v1/projects`,
    JSON.stringify(projectData),
    { headers: { ...headers, 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } }
  );
  
  check(res, {
    'project created': (r) => r.status === 201,
    'has project id': (r) => r.json('id') !== undefined
  });
  
  return res.json('id');
}

function executeLLMFlow(token, projectId, prompt) {
  const payload = {
    projectId,
    prompt,
    model: 'gpt-4',
    temperature: 0.7
  };
  
  const res = http.post(
    `${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/v1/llm/execute`,
    JSON.stringify(payload),
    { headers: { ...headers, 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } }
  );
  
  check(res, {
    'llm execution success': (r) => r.status === 200,
    'has valid response': (r) => r.json('result') !== undefined,
    'response time < 3s': (r) => r.timings.duration < 3000
  });
  
  return res.json('result');
}

// Cenário principal
export default function () {
  const user = testUsers[Math.floor(Math.random() * testUsers.length)];
  
  group('Cenário Completo - Usuário Ativo', () => {
    // 1. Login
    const token = login(user);
    if (!token) {
      console.error(`Login failed for user: ${user.email}`);
      return;
    }
    
    // 2. Dashboard
    const dashboardRes = http.get(
      `${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/v1/dashboard`,
      { headers: { ...headers, 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } }
    );
    check(dashboardRes, { 'dashboard loaded': (r) => r.status === 200 });
    
    // 3. Criar projeto
    const projectData = {
      name: `Test Project ${Date.now()}`,
      type: 'automation',
      components: ['llm', 'database', 'api']
    };
    const projectId = createProject(token, projectData);
    
    // 4. Executar fluxo IA
    if (projectId) {
      const prompt = "Generate a test automation script for login flow";
      executeLLMFlow(token, projectId, prompt);
    }
    
    // 5. Listar projetos
    const projectsRes = http.get(
      `${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/v1/projects`,
      { headers: { ...headers, 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } }
    );
    check(projectsRes, { 'projects listed': (r) => r.status === 200 });
    
    // 6. Logout
    const logoutRes = http.post(
      `${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/v1/auth/logout`,
      null,
      { headers: { ...headers, 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } }
    );
    check(logoutRes, { 'logout successful': (r) => r.status === 200 });
  });
  
  sleep(Math.random() * 2 + 1); // Think time
}

// Gerar relatório
export function handleSummary(data) {
  return {
    'stdout': textSummary(data, { indent: ' ', enableColors: true }),
    'reports/performance/load_test_summary.html': htmlReport(data),
    'reports/performance/load_test.json': JSON.stringify(data)
  };
}
```

### 1.3 Script de Teste de Stress

```javascript
// tests/performance/k6/stress_test.js
import http from 'k6/http';
import { check, sleep } from 'k6';
import { Counter, Rate, Trend } from 'k6/metrics';

// Métricas
const errorCounter = new Counter('errors_total');
const successRate = new Rate('success_rate');
const responseTime = new Trend('response_time_ms');

export const options = {
  stages: [
    { duration: '2m', target: 100 },    // Ramp up
    { duration: '5m', target: 500 },    // Carga média
    { duration: '3m', target: 1000 },   // Alta carga
    { duration: '2m', target: 2000 },   // Pico
    { duration: '5m', target: 2000 },   // Sustentar pico
    { duration: '2m', target: 100 },    // Ramp down
  ],
  thresholds: {
    'http_req_failed': ['rate<0.05'],
    'http_req_duration': ['p(95)<5000'],
  },
  noConnectionReuse: true, // Testar novas conexões
  userAgent: 'DIYAPP-Stress-Test/1.0'
};

export default function () {
  const testCases = [
    {
      name: 'heavy_llm_request',
      method: 'POST',
      url: `${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/v1/llm/complex`,
      body: JSON.stringify({
        prompt: 'A'.repeat(5000), // Payload grande
        model: 'gpt-4',
        max_tokens: 4000
      }),
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }
    },
    {
      name: 'concurrent_database',
      method: 'GET',
      url: `${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/v1/data/analytics?deep=true`
    },
    {
      name: 'file_upload_sim',
      method: 'POST',
      url: `${__ENV.BASE_URL}/api/v1/files/process`,
      body: JSON.stringify({ size: 10485760 }), // 10MB
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }
    }
  ];
  
  const testCase = testCases[Math.floor(Math.random() * testCases.length)];
  
  const startTime = Date.now();
  const res = http.request(testCase.method, testCase.url, testCase.body, {
    headers: testCase.headers
  });
  const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
  
  const isSuccess = check(res, {
    [`${testCase.name} status`]: (r) => r.status >= 200 && r.status < 500,
    [`${testCase.name} response time`]: (r) => r.timings.duration < 10000
  });
  
  if (isSuccess) {
    successRate.add(1);
    responseTime.add(duration);
  } else {
    errorCounter.add(1);
    successRate.add(0);
    console.error(`Stress test failed: ${testCase.name}`, res.status);
  }
  
  sleep(Math.random() * 0.5); // Intervalo mínimo
}
```

/**
 * Roteiro de Chaos Engineering - DIYAPP V12

const ChaosTestPlan = {
