  grid-column: span 12;
  margin-top: ${({ theme }) => theme.spacing.xl};
`;

export const Dashboard: React.FC = () => {
  const theme = useTheme();
  const { data, isLoading, error, refetch } = useDashboardData();
  const [activeView, setActiveView] = useState<'overview' | 'detailed'>('overview');

  if (isLoading) {
    return <LoadingState message="Carregando dashboard..." />;
  }

  if (error) {
    return (
      <ErrorState
        error={error}
        onRetry={refetch}
        title="Erro ao carregar dashboard"
      />
    );
  }

  return (
    <DashboardContainer>
      <DashboardHeader
        title="DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core"
        subtitle="Dashboard de monitoramento e gestão"
        activeView={activeView}
        onViewChange={setActiveView}
        lastUpdated={data?.lastUpdated}
      />
      
      <DashboardGrid>
        <MetricsSection>
          <MetricsGrid metrics={data?.metrics || []} />
        </MetricsSection>
        
        <KanbanSection>
          <KanbanBoard
            columns={data?.kanbanColumns || []}
            onTaskMove={handleTaskMove}
            onTaskAdd={handleTaskAdd}
          />
        </KanbanSection>
        
        <ChartSection>
          <ActivityChart
            data={data?.activityData || []}
            timeRange="7d"
            onTimeRangeChange={handleTimeRangeChange}
          />
        </ChartSection>
      </DashboardGrid>
    </DashboardContainer>
  );
};

// Handlers com tratamento de erro explícito

};

    // Implementação real com API

    throw error;
  }
};

const handleTimeRangeChange = (range: string) => {
  // Implementação para atualizar dados do gráfico
  console.log('Time range changed to:', range);
};

```typescript
// src/hooks/useDashboardData.ts
import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { dashboardService } from '../services/dashboardService';

interface DashboardData {
  metrics: Metric[];
  kanbanColumns: KanbanColumn[];
  activityData: ActivityDataPoint[];
  lastUpdated: string;
}

interface Metric {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  value: number;
  change: number;
  changeType: 'positive' | 'negative' | 'neutral';
  format: 'number' | 'percentage' | 'currency';
}

interface KanbanColumn {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  tasks: KanbanTask[];
}

interface KanbanTask {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  description?: string;
  assignee?: string;
  priority: 'low' | 'medium' | 'high';
  tags: string[];
}

interface ActivityDataPoint {
  date: string;
  value: number;
  category: string;
}

export const useDashboardData = () => {
  const [data, setData] = useState<DashboardData | null>(null);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<Error | null>(null);

  const fetchData = useCallback(async () => {
    setIsLoading(true);
    setError(null);

    try {
      const response = await dashboardService.getDashboardData();
      
      // Validação dos dados recebidos
      if (!response || !response.metrics || !response.kanbanColumns) {
        throw new Error('Dados do dashboard inválidos');
      }
      
      setData(response);
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err instanceof Error ? err : new Error('Erro desconhecido'));
      console.error('Failed to fetch dashboard data:', err);
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchData();
    
    // Polling para atualização automática (opcional)
    const intervalId = setInterval(fetchData, 30000); // 30 segundos
    
    return () => clearInterval(intervalId);
  }, [fetchData]);

  const refetch = useCallback(() => {
    fetchData();
  }, [fetchData]);

  return { data, isLoading, error, refetch };
};
```

```typescript
// src/services/dashboardService.ts
import { apiClient } from './apiClient';

class DashboardService {
  private baseUrl = '/api/dashboard';

  async getDashboardData() {
    try {
      const response = await apiClient.get(this.baseUrl);
      return this.transformDashboardData(response.data);
    } catch (error) {
      // Log para monitoramento
      console.error('DashboardService.getDashboardData failed:', error);
      throw this.handleApiError(error);
    }
  }

  async updateMetric(metricId: string, value: number) {
    try {
      const response = await apiClient.patch(`${this.baseUrl}/metrics/${metricId}`, { value });
      return response.data;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(`DashboardService.updateMetric failed for ${metricId}:`, error);
      throw this.handleApiError(error);
    }
  }

  async moveTask(taskId: string, targetColumnId: string) {
    try {
      const response = await apiClient.post(`${this.baseUrl}/tasks/${taskId}/move`, {
        targetColumnId,
      });
      return response.data;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(`DashboardService.moveTask failed for ${taskId}:`, error);
      throw this.handleApiError(error);
    }
  }

  private transformDashboardData(rawData: any) {
    // Transformação e validação dos dados da API
    return {
      metrics: rawData.metrics?.map(this.transformMetric) || [],
      kanbanColumns: rawData.kanbanColumns?.map(this.transformKanbanColumn) || [],
      activityData: rawData.activityData?.map(this.transformActivityData) || [],
      lastUpdated: rawData.lastUpdated || new Date().toISOString(),
    };
  }

  private transformMetric(rawMetric: any) {
    return {
      id: rawMetric.id,
      title: rawMetric.title,
      value: Number(rawMetric.value) || 0,
      change: Number(rawMetric.change) || 0,
      changeType: ['positive', 'negative', 'neutral'].includes(rawMetric.changeType)
        ? rawMetric.changeType
        : 'neutral',
      format: ['number', 'percentage', 'currency'].includes(rawMetric.format)
        ? rawMetric.format
        : 'number',
    };
  }

  private handleApiError(error: any): Error {
    if (error.response) {
      // Erro da API
      switch (error.response.status) {
        case 401:
          return new Error('Autenticação necessária');
        case 403:
          return new Error('Permissão negada');
        case 404:
          return new Error('Recurso não encontrado');
        case 429:
          return new Error('Muitas requisições. Tente novamente mais tarde.');
        case 500:
          return new Error('Erro interno do servidor');
        default:
          return new Error(`Erro ${error.response.status}: ${error.response.data?.message || 'Erro desconhecido'}`);
      }
    } else if (error.request) {
      // Erro de rede
      return new Error('Erro de conexão. Verifique sua internet.');
    } else {
      // Erro na configuração da requisição
      return new Error('Erro na configuração da requisição');
    }
  }
}

export const dashboardService = new DashboardService();
```

```typescript
// src/services/apiClient.ts
import axios from 'axios';

// Configuração centralizada do Axios com interceptors
const apiClient = axios.create({
  baseURL: process.env.REACT_APP_API_BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:3000',
  timeout: 10000, // 10 segundos
  headers: {
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  },
});

// Request interceptor para adicionar token de autenticação
apiClient.interceptors.request.use(
  (config) => {
    const token = localStorage.getItem('auth_token');
    if (token) {
      config.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${token}`;
    }
    return config;
  },
  (error) => {
    return Promise.reject(error);
  }
);

// Response interceptor para tratamento global de erros
apiClient.interceptors.response.use(
  (response) => response,
  async (error) => {
    const originalRequest = error.config;

    // Tratamento de token expirado (refresh token)
    if (error.response?.status === 401 && !originalRequest._retry) {
      originalRequest._retry = true;
      
      try {
        const refreshToken = localStorage.getItem('refresh_token');
        const response = await axios.post('/api/auth/refresh', { refreshToken });
        
        const { accessToken } = response.data;
        localStorage.setItem('auth_token', accessToken);
        
        originalRequest.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${accessToken}`;
        return apiClient(originalRequest);
      } catch (refreshError) {
        // Refresh falhou, redirecionar para login
        localStorage.removeItem('auth_token');
        localStorage.removeItem('refresh_token');
        window.location.href = '/login';
        return Promise.reject(refreshError);
      }
    }

    return Promise.reject(error);
  }
);

// Retry com backoff exponencial
export const fetchWithRetry = async (
  fn: ()

services:
  # Banco de dados V12 (PostgreSQL)

## 3. Modelo de Dados PostgreSQL V12

### `src/database/migrations/v12/001_init_schema.sql`

```sql
-- Schema principal V12
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS app;
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS analytics;
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS audit;

-- Tabelas principais da aplicação
CREATE TABLE app.users (
    user_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    username VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    full_name VARCHAR(255),
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    last_login_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    migration_id VARCHAR(100), -- ID da V11 para rastreabilidade
    migration_batch_id UUID
);

CREATE TABLE app.conversations (
    conversation_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES app.users(user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    title VARCHAR(500),
    context JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    is_archived BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    token_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    cost_estimate DECIMAL(10, 6) DEFAULT 0,
    migration_id VARCHAR(100),
    migration_batch_id UUID,
    INDEX idx_conversations_user (user_id),
    INDEX idx_conversations_created (created_at)
);

CREATE TABLE app.messages (
    message_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    conversation_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES app.conversations(conversation_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    role VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL CHECK (role IN ('user', 'assistant', 'system')),
    content TEXT NOT NULL,
    tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    model_used VARCHAR(100),
    cost DECIMAL(10, 6),
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    migration_id VARCHAR(100),
    INDEX idx_messages_conversation (conversation_id),
    INDEX idx_messages_created (created_at)
);

-- Tabelas de analytics
CREATE TABLE analytics.daily_active_users (
    date DATE PRIMARY KEY,
    total_users INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    active_users INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    new_users INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    returning_users INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    avg_session_duration INTERVAL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE analytics.feature_usage (
    feature_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    feature_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    user_id UUID REFERENCES app.users(user_id),
    usage_count INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
    first_used_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    last_used_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    UNIQUE(feature_name, user_id)
);

CREATE TABLE analytics.llm_metrics (
    metric_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    total_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    prompt_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    completion_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    total_cost DECIMAL(10, 6) NOT NULL,
    request_duration_ms INTEGER NOT NULL,
    user_id UUID REFERENCES app.users(user_id),
    conversation_id UUID REFERENCES app.conversations(conversation_id),
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_llm_metrics_created (created_at),
    INDEX idx_llm_metrics_model (model_name, provider)
);

-- Tabelas de auditoria
CREATE TABLE audit.data_migration_log (
    log_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    batch_id UUID NOT NULL,
    source_table VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    target_table VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    records_migrated INTEGER NOT NULL,
    migration_started_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    migration_completed_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'in_progress', 'completed', 'failed')),
    error_message TEXT,
    INDEX idx_migration_batch (batch_id),
    INDEX idx_migration_status (status)
);

CREATE TABLE audit.data_quality_log (
    quality_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    check_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    table_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    check_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL CHECK (check_type IN ('completeness', 'uniqueness', 'validity', 'consistency')),
    expected_value NUMERIC,
    actual_value NUMERIC,
    threshold NUMERIC,
    passed BOOLEAN NOT NULL,
    checked_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    details JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    INDEX idx_quality_table (table_name),
    INDEX idx_quality_passed (passed, checked_at)
);

-- Funções de trigger para updated_at
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    NEW.updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP;
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

-- Triggers para updated_at
CREATE TRIGGER update_users_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON app.users
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

CREATE TRIGGER update_conversations_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON app.conversations
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

-- Views materializadas para performance
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW analytics.user_activity_summary AS
SELECT 
    u.user_id,
    u.email,
    u.created_at as user_created_at,
    COUNT(DISTINCT DATE(c.created_at)) as active_days,
    COUNT(DISTINCT c.conversation_id) as total_conversations,
    SUM(m.token_count) as total_tokens_used,
    MAX(c.updated_at) as last_activity_at
FROM app.users u
LEFT JOIN app.conversations c ON u.user_id = c.user_id
LEFT JOIN app.messages m ON c.conversation_id = m.conversation_id
GROUP BY u.user_id, u.email, u.created_at;

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX idx_user_activity_summary ON analytics.user_activity_summary(user_id);

-- Refresh da view materializada
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE analytics.refresh_user_activity_summary()
LANGUAGE plpgsql
AS $$
BEGIN
    REFRESH MATERIALIZED VIEW CONCURRENTLY analytics.user_activity_summary;
END;
$$;
```

## 4. Pipeline de Migração V11 → V12

### `src/etl/pipelines/migration_pipeline.py`

```python
import asyncio
import logging
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any
import uuid
import psycopg2
from psycopg2.extras import RealDictCursor
from psycopg2.pool import SimpleConnectionPool
from redis import Redis
import json
from dataclasses import dataclass
from enum import Enum

from src.database.connection import get_db_pool, get_redis_client
from src.utils.migration_helpers import DataValidator, BatchProcessor
from src.utils.logging_config import setup_logging

logger = setup_logging(__name__)

class MigrationStatus(Enum):
    PENDING = "pending"
    IN_PROGRESS = "in_progress"
    COMPLETED = "completed"
    FAILED = "failed"

@dataclass
class MigrationConfig:
    batch_size: int = 1000
    max_retries: int = 3
    retry_delay: int = 5  # seconds
    validation_enabled: bool = True
    dry_run: bool = False

class MigrationPipeline:
    def __init__(self, config: Optional[MigrationConfig] = None):
        self.config = config or MigrationConfig()
        self.batch_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
        self.v11_pool = None
        self.v12_pool = None
        self.redis = None
        self.validator = DataValidator()
        self.processor = BatchProcessor()
        
    async def initialize(self):
        """Initialize database connections"""
        try:
            # Pool para V11 (legado)
            self.v11_pool = SimpleConnectionPool(
                minconn=1,
                maxconn=10,
                host="postgres-v11",


### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
```javascript
// DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Technical Architecture Specification
// Arquitetura de Microsserviços, Padrões de Código, CI/CD e Observabilidade
// Tech Lead: Squad Autônoma de IA - V12 Core

// ============================================================================
// ARQUITETURA DE MICROSSERVIÇOS E CONTAINERS
// ============================================================================

// ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços para DIYAPP V12
// Data: 2024-01-15
// Status: Aceita
// Autores: Tech Lead + Especialista Infra + Especialista LLM

/**
 * CONTEXTO:
 * DIYAPP evoluiu de monólito para arquitetura distribuída com 50k+ usuários ativos.
 * Necessidade de: escalabilidade independente, deploy contínuo, resiliência e observabilidade.
 * Forças: time distribuído, múltiplas squads autônomas, necessidade de deploy independente.
 */

/**
 * DECISÃO:
 * Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços baseada em containers Docker com Kubernetes.
 * Cada microsserviço é uma unidade de deploy independente com responsabilidade única.
 * Comunicação via gRPC para serviços internos, REST para APIs públicas.
 */

/**
 * ESTRUTURA DE MICROSSERVIÇOS:
 */
const microservicesArchitecture = {
  // Core Services
  'user-service': {
    responsibility: 'Gestão de usuários, autenticação, autorização',
    techStack: ['Node.js 18', 'Express', 'PostgreSQL', 'Redis'],
    endpoints: ['/api/v1/users/**', '/api/v1/auth/**'],
    port: 3001,
    replicas: 3,
    healthCheck: '/health'
  },
  
  'content-service': {
    responsibility: 'Gestão de conteúdo, posts, comentários, mídia',
    techStack: ['Node.js 18', 'Fastify', 'MongoDB', 'S3'],
    endpoints: ['/api/v1/content/**', '/api/v1/media/**'],
    port: 3002,
    replicas: 4,
    healthCheck: '/health'
  },
  
  'ai-orchestrator': {
    responsibility: 'Orquestração de modelos LLM, prompts, inferência',
    techStack: ['Python 3.11', 'FastAPI', 'Redis', 'PostgreSQL'],
    endpoints: ['/api/v1/ai/**', '/api/v1/prompts/**'],
    port: 3003,
    replicas: 2,
    healthCheck: '/health'
  },
  
  'notification-service': {
    responsibility: 'Notificações em tempo real, email, push, WhatsApp',
    techStack: ['Node.js 18', 'Socket.io', 'RabbitMQ', 'Redis'],
    endpoints: ['/api/v1/notifications/**', '/ws/**'],
    port: 3004,
    replicas: 2,
    healthCheck: '/health'
  },
  
  'payment-service': {
    responsibility: 'Processamento de pagamentos, assinaturas, invoices',
    techStack: ['Go 1.21', 'Gin', 'PostgreSQL', 'Stripe SDK'],
    endpoints: ['/api/v1/payments/**', '/api/v1/subscriptions/**'],
    port: 3005,
    replicas: 2,
    healthCheck: '/health'
  },
  
  // Infrastructure Services
  'api-gateway': {
    responsibility: 'Gateway único, rate limiting, CORS, SSL termination',
    techStack: ['Nginx', 'Lua', 'Redis'],
    endpoints: ['/*'],
    port: 443,
    replicas: 2,
    healthCheck: '/status'
  },
  
  'service-discovery': {
    responsibility: 'Registry de serviços, load balancing, failover',
    techStack: ['Consul', 'Envoy'],
    endpoints: [],
    port: 8500,
    replicas: 3,
    healthCheck: '/v1/agent/self'
  }
};

/**
 * OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
 * - Opção A: Monólito modularizado — Prós: Simplicidade inicial. Contras: Escalabilidade limitada, deploy único.
 * - Opção B: Microsserviços com Docker Swarm — Prós: Mais simples que K8s. Contras: Menos recursos, comunidade menor.
 * - Opção C: Microsserviços com Kubernetes — Prós: Padrão de mercado, auto-scaling, rich ecosystem. Contras: Complexidade inicial.
 * 
 * Opção escolhida: C — Justificativa: Escalabilidade comprovada, suporte a CI/CD nativo, mercado maduro.
 */

/**
 * CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
 * Positivas: Escalabilidade independente, deploy contínuo, resiliência, polyglot persistence.
 * Negativas: Complexidade operacional, latência de rede, necessidade de observabilidade robusta.
 * Riscos: Distributed tracing complexo, consistência eventual, debugging distribuído.
 */

// ============================================================================
// PADRÕES DE CÓDIGO E ENGINEERING STANDARDS
// ============================================================================

// ADR-002: Padrões de Código e Estrutura de Projeto
// Data: 2024-01-15
// Status: Aceita

const engineeringStandards = {
  // Estrutura de Projeto
  projectStructure: `
    src/
    ├── controllers/     # Controladores HTTP
    ├── services/        # Lógica de negócio
    ├── repositories/    # Acesso a dados
    ├── models/          # Modelos de dados/entidades
    ├── middleware/      # Middleware Express/Fastify
    ├── utils/           # Utilitários compartilhados
    ├── config/          # Configurações
    ├── tests/           # Testes
    │   ├── unit/        # Testes unitários
    │   ├── integration/ # Testes de integração
    │   └── e2e/         # Testes end-to-end
    └── types/           # TypeScript definitions
  `,
  
  // Convenções de Nomenclatura
  namingConventions: {
    files: 'kebab-case (ex: user-service.js)',
    classes: 'PascalCase (ex: UserController)',
    functions: 'camelCase (ex: getUserById)',
    constants: 'UPPER_SNAKE_CASE (ex: MAX_RETRY_COUNT)',
    variables: 'camelCase (ex: userData)',
    interfaces: 'PascalCase com prefixo I (ex: IUser)',
    types: 'PascalCase com sufixo Type (ex: UserType)'
  },
  
  // Padrões de Commit
  commitConventions: {
    format: 'Conventional Commits',
    types: ['feat', 'fix', 'docs', 'style', 'refactor', 'test', 'chore'],
    example: 'feat(auth): add JWT authentication middleware',
    scope: 'Deve indicar o módulo/componente afetado'
  },
  
  // Qualidade de Código
  codeQuality: {
    linting: 'ESLint com Airbnb Base + Prettier',
    testCoverage: 'Mínimo 80% coverage',
    complexity: 'Cyclomatic complexity máxima 10 por função',
    fileSize: 'Máximo 400 linhas por arquivo',
    functionSize: 'Máximo 50 linhas por função'
  },
  
  // Segurança
  securityStandards: {
    authentication: 'JWT com refresh tokens',
    authorization: 'RBAC (Role-Based Access Control)',
    inputValidation: 'Joi ou Zod para todas as entradas',
    secrets: 'Armazenar em HashiCorp Vault ou AWS Secrets Manager',
    logging: 'Nunca logar dados sensíveis (senhas, tokens, PII)'
  },
  
  // Performance
  performanceStandards: {
    database: 'Índices para queries frequentes, evitar N+1',
    caching: 'Redis para cache de 1º nível, CDN para estáticos',
    pagination: 'Cursor-based pagination para listas grandes',
    compression: 'Gzip/Brotli para todas as respostas HTTP',
    timeout: 'Timeout máximo de 30s para requests externos'
  }
};

// ============================================================================
// CI/CD PIPELINE
// ============================================================================

// ADR-003: Pipeline de CI/CD para Deploy Contínuo
// Data: 2024-01-15
// Status: Aceita

/**
 * Pipeline em 4 estágios: Build → Test → Deploy Staging → Deploy Production
 * Git Flow com branches: main (production), staging, feature/*
 */

const ciCdPipeline = {
  // Configuração do GitHub Actions
  githubActionsConfig: `
name: CI/CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, staging]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  build-and-test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: '18'
          cache: 'npm'
      
      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci
      
      - name: Lint code
        run: npm run lint
      
      - name: Run unit tests
        run: npm test -- --coverage
      
      - name: Upload coverage
        uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
        with:
          file: ./coverage/lcov.info
      
      - name: Build Docker image
        run: docker build -t diyapp/${{ github.event.repository.name }}:${{ github.sha }} .
      
      - name: Push to Container Registry
        run: |
          echo "${{ secrets.DOCKER_PASSWORD }}" | docker login -u "${{ secrets.DOCKER_USERNAME }}" --password-stdin
          docker push diyapp/${{ github.event.repository.name }}:${{ github.sha }}

  deploy-staging:
    needs: build-and-test
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/staging'
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Deploy to Staging
        run: |
          kubectl config use-context staging
          kubectl set image deployment/${{ github.event.repository.name }} ${{ github.event.repository.name }}=diyapp/${{ github.event.repository.name }}:${{ github.sha }}
          kubectl rollout status deployment/${{ github.event.repository.name }}

  deploy-production:
    needs: build-and-test
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Manual approval
        uses: trstringer/manual-approval@v1
        with:
          secret: ${{ github.TOKEN }}
          approvers: tech-lead, squad-leader
          minimum-approvals: 2
      
      - name: Deploy to Production
        run: |
          kubectl config use-context production
          kubectl set image deployment/${{ github.event.repository.name }} ${{ github.event.repository.name }}=diyapp/${{ github.event.repository.name }}:${{ github.sha }}
          kubectl rollout status deployment/${{ github.event.repository.name }}
  `,
  
  // Estratégia de Deploy
  deploymentStrategy: {
    staging: 'Blue-Green Deployment',
    production: 'Rolling Update com health checks',
    rollback: 'Automático se health check falhar por 3 minutos',
    canary: '5% do tráfego para nova versão por 1 hora'
  },
  
  // Versionamento
  versioning: {
    api: 'Semantic Versioning (v1.2.3)',
    docker: 'Git SHA como tag + latest para staging',
    helm: 'Chart version incrementado em cada deploy'
  }
};

// ============================================================================

// ADR-004: Stack de Observabilidade para Sistema Distribuído
// Data: 2024-01-15
// Status: Aceita

const observabilityStack = {
  // Logging
  logging: {
    standard: 'Structured JSON logs',
    levels: ['error', 'warn', 'info', 'debug', 'trace'],
    fields: {
      mandatory: ['timestamp', 'level', 'service', 'correlationId', 'message'],
      optional: ['userId', 'requestId', 'durationMs', 'httpMethod', 'httpStatus']
    },
    aggregation: 'Fluentd → Elasticsearch → Kibana',
    retention: '30 dias para produção, 7 dias para staging'
  },
  
  // Metrics
  metrics: {
    collection: 'Prometheus + Node Exporter',
    exposition: '/metrics endpoint em cada serviço',
    keyMetrics: {
      application: ['http_requests_total', 'http_request_duration_seconds', 'error_rate'],
      business: ['user_signups_total', 'payments_processed_total', 'active_users'],
      infrastructure: ['cpu_usage', 'memory_usage', 'disk_io', 'network_bytes']
    },
    visualization: 'Grafana dashboards',
    alerting: 'Alertmanager com regras baseadas em SLOs'
  },
  
  // Distributed Tracing
  tracing: {
    implementation: 'OpenTelemetry SDK',
    propagation: 'W3C Trace Context',
    exporters: ['Jaeger', 'Zipkin'],
    sampling: 'Head-based sampling (10% para produção)',
    spans: {
      mandatory: 'HTTP requests, DB queries, external API calls',
      optional: 'Business logic spans'
    }
  },
  
  // Health Checks
  healthChecks: {
    liveness: '/health/live - verifica se app está rodando',
    readiness: '/health/ready - verifica dependências (DB, Redis, etc)',
    startup: '/health/startup - verifica inicialização completa',
    frequency: 'Kubernetes verifica a cada 30s',
    timeout: '5 segundos máximo'
  },
  
  // SLOs (Service Level Objectives)
  slos: {
    availability: '99.95% uptime (≤ 4.38h downtime/ano)',
    latency: 'P95 < 500ms para APIs críticas',
    errorRate: 'Error budget de 0.1% (99.9% success rate)',
    throughput: 'Capacidade para 10k RPS por serviço'
  }
};

// Dockerfile de referência para serviços Node.js
const dockerfileTemplate = `
# DIYAPP V12 - Dockerfile Template
# Tech Lead Approved - ADR-005

FROM node:18-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

# Instalar dependências
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copiar código fonte
COPY . .

# Criar usuário não-root
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs && \
    adduser -S nodejs -u 1001

USER nodejs

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=5s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \\
  CMD node health-check.js

# Expor porta
EXPOSE 3000

# Comando de inicialização
CMD ["node", "src/server.js"]
`;

// Kubernetes Deployment Template
const kubernetesDeployment = `
# DIYAPP V12 - Kubernetes Deployment Template
# Tech Lead Approved - ADR-006

apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: {{SERVICE_NAME}}
  namespace: {{NAMESPACE}}
  labels:
    app: {{SERVICE_NAME}}
    version: {{VERSION}}
spec:
  replicas: {{REPLICAS}}
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: {{SERVICE_NAME}}
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate:
      maxSurge: 1
      maxUnavailable: 0
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: {{SERVICE_NAME}}
        version: {{VERSION}}
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: {{SERVICE_NAME}}
        image: {{IMAGE}}:{{TAG}}
        ports:
        - containerPort: {{PORT}}
        env:
        - name: NODE_ENV
          value: "production"
        - name: SERVICE_NAME
          value: "{{SERVICE_NAME}}"
        - name: OTEL_SERVICE_NAME
          value: "{{SERVICE_NAME}}"
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "256Mi"
            cpu: "100m"
          limits:
            memory: "512Mi"
            cpu: "500m"
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health/live
            port: {{PORT}}
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health/ready
            port: {{PORT}}
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
        startupProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health/startup
            port: {{PORT}}
          failureThreshold: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: {{SERVICE_NAME}}
  namespace: {{NAMESPACE}}
spec:
  selector:
    app: {{SERVICE_NAME}}
  ports:
  - port: 80
    targetPort: {{PORT}}
    protocol: TCP
  type: ClusterIP
`;

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Sistema de Design

Vou criar um sistema de design completo com tokens, componentes atômicos e protótipos interativos para fluxos críticos.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```

  10: '2.5rem',    // 40px

  16: '4rem',      // 64px
  20: '5rem',      // 80px

  32: '8rem',      // 128px
  40: '10rem',     // 160px
  48: '12rem',     // 192px
  64: '16rem',     // 256px

  xs: '320px',
  sm: '640px',
  md: '768px',
  lg: '1024px',
  xl: '1280px',
  '2xl': '1536px'

```javascript
// src/design-tokens/shadows.js
export const shadows = {
  xs: '0 1px 2px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.05)',
  sm: '0 1px 3px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 1px 2px -1px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
  base: '0 4px 6px -1px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 2px 4px -2px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
  md: '0 10px 15px -3px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 4px 6px -4px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
  lg: '0 20px 25px -5px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 8px 10px -6px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
  xl: '0 25px 50px -12px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.25)',
  inner: 'inset 0 2px 4px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.05)',
  none: 'none'
};
```

## 2. Componentes Atômicos (src/components/atoms/)

### Button Component
```javascript
// src/components/atoms/Button/Button.js
import { colors, typography, spacing, shadows } from '../../design-tokens';

export class Button {
  constructor(options = {}) {
    this.variant = options.variant || 'primary';
    this.size = options.size || 'medium';
    this.state = options.state || 'default';
    this.icon = options.icon || null;
    this.label = options.label || 'Button';
    this.onClick = options.onClick || (() => {});
    this.disabled = options.disabled || false;
    this.loading = options.loading || false;
  }

  getStyles() {
    const baseStyles = {
      fontFamily: typography.fontFamily.sans,
      fontWeight: typography.fontWeight.medium,
      borderRadius: '0.5rem',
      border: 'none',
      cursor: 'pointer',
      display: 'inline-flex',
      alignItems: 'center',
      justifyContent: 'center',
      gap: spacing[2],
      transition: 'all 150ms cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
      outline: 'none',
      position: 'relative',
      overflow: 'hidden'
    };

    const sizeStyles = {
      small: {
        fontSize: typography.fontSize.sm,
        padding: `${spacing[1]} ${spacing[3]}`,
        height: '2rem'
      },
      medium: {
        fontSize: typography.fontSize.base,
        padding: `${spacing[2]} ${spacing[4]}`,
        height: '2.5rem'
      },
      large: {
        fontSize: typography.fontSize.lg,
        padding: `${spacing[3]} ${spacing[6]}`,
        height: '3rem'
      }
    };

    const variantStyles = {
      primary: {
        default: {
          backgroundColor: colors.primary[600],
          color: colors.text.inverse,
          boxShadow: shadows.sm
        },
        hover: {
          backgroundColor: colors.primary[700],
          boxShadow: shadows.base
        },
        focus: {
          boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${colors.primary[200]}`
        },
        active: {
          backgroundColor: colors.primary[800]
        },
        disabled: {
          backgroundColor: colors.neutral[300],
          color: colors.neutral[500],
          cursor: 'not-allowed'
        }
      },
      secondary: {
        default: {
          backgroundColor: colors.neutral[100],
          color: colors.text.primary,
          border: `1px solid ${colors.border.medium}`,
          boxShadow: shadows.xs
        },
        hover: {
          backgroundColor: colors.neutral[200],
          boxShadow: shadows.sm
        },
        focus: {
          boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${colors.neutral[300]}`
        },
        active: {
          backgroundColor: colors.neutral[300]
        },
        disabled: {
          backgroundColor: colors.neutral[100],
          color: colors.neutral[400],
          borderColor: colors.neutral[300],
          cursor: 'not-allowed'
        }
      },
      ghost: {
        default: {
          backgroundColor: 'transparent',
          color: colors.text.primary,
          border: '1px solid transparent'
        },
        hover: {
          backgroundColor: colors.neutral[100]
        },
        focus: {
          backgroundColor: colors.neutral[100],
          boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${colors.neutral[300]}`
        },
        active: {
          backgroundColor: colors.neutral[200]
        },
        disabled: {
          color: colors.neutral[400],
          cursor: 'not-allowed'
        }
      }
    };

    return { ...baseStyles, ...sizeStyles[this.size], ...variantStyles[this.variant][this.state] };
  }

  render() {
    const styles = this.getStyles();
    const button = document.createElement('button');
    
    Object.assign(button.style, styles);
    button.textContent = this.label;
    button.disabled = this.disabled || this.loading;
    
    if (this.loading) {
      const spinner = document.createElement('span');
      spinner.className = 'button-spinner';
      spinner.style.cssText = `
        width: 1rem;
        height: 1rem;
        border: 2px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.3);
        border-radius: 50%;
        border-top-color: white;
        animation: spin 1s linear infinite;
      `;
      button.appendChild(spinner);
    }
    
    if (this.icon) {
      const icon = document.createElement('span');
      icon.textContent = this.icon;
      button.prepend(icon);
    }
    
    button.addEventListener('click', this.onClick);
    
    // Add hover effects
    button.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
      if (!this.disabled && !this.loading) {
        Object.assign(button.style, this.getStylesForState('hover'));
      }
    });
    
    button.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
      if (!this.disabled && !this.loading) {
        Object.assign(button.style, this.getStylesForState('default'));
      }
    });
    
    return button;
  }

  getStylesForState(state) {
    // Return styles for specific state
    const variant = this.variantStyles[this.variant][state];
    return variant || {};
  }
}
```

### Input Component
```javascript
// src/components/atoms/Input/Input.js
import { colors, typography, spacing } from '../../design-tokens';

export class Input {
  constructor(options = {}) {
    this.type = options.type || 'text';
    this.placeholder = options.placeholder || '';
    this.value = options.value || '';
    this.label = options.label || '';
    this.helperText = options.helperText || '';
    this.error = options.error || '';
    this.disabled = options.disabled || false;
    this.required = options.required || false;
    this.icon = options.icon || null;
    this.onChange = options.onChange || (() => {});
    this.onFocus = options.onFocus || (() => {});
    this.onBlur = options.onBlur || (() => {});
  }

  getStyles() {
    return {
      container: {
        display: 'flex',
        flexDirection: 'column',
        gap: spacing[1]
      },
      label: {
        fontFamily: typography.fontFamily.sans,
        fontSize: typography.fontSize.sm,
        fontWeight: typography.fontWeight.medium,
        color: colors.text.primary,
        marginBottom: spacing[1]
      },
      inputWrapper: {
        position: 'relative',
        display: 'flex',
        alignItems: 'center'
      },
      input: {
        fontFamily: typography.fontFamily.sans,
        fontSize: typography.fontSize.base,
        width: '100%',
        padding: `${spacing[2]} ${spacing[3]}`,
        paddingLeft: this.icon ? spacing[10] : spacing[3],
        borderRadius: '0.5rem',
        border: `1px solid ${this.error ? colors.semantic.error[500] : colors.border.medium}`,
        backgroundColor: this.disabled ? colors.neutral[100] : colors.background.primary,
        color: colors.text.primary,
        outline: 'none',
        transition: 'border-color 150ms, box-shadow 150ms',
        '&:focus': {
          borderColor: this.error ? colors.semantic.error[600] : colors.primary[500],
          boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${this.error ? colors.semantic.error[100] : colors.primary[100]}`
        },
        '&:disabled': {
          backgroundColor: colors.neutral[100],
          color: colors.text.disabled,
          cursor: 'not-allowed'
        }
      },
      icon: {
        position: 'absolute',
        left: spacing[3],
        color: colors.text.tertiary
      },
      helperText: {
        fontFamily: typography.fontFamily.sans,
        fontSize: typography.fontSize.sm,
        color: this.error ? colors.semantic.error[600] : colors.text.secondary,
        marginTop: spacing[1]
      }
    };
  }

  render() {
    const styles = this.getStyles();
    const container = document.createElement('div');
    Object.assign(container.style, styles.container

// 3. src/config/index.ts
import dotenv from 'dotenv';
import { z } from 'zod';

dotenv.config();

const configSchema = z.object({
  NODE_ENV: z.enum(['development', 'production', 'test']).default('development'),
  PORT: z.string().transform(Number).default('3000'),
  
  // Database
  DB_HOST: z.string().default('localhost'),
  DB_PORT: z.string().transform(Number).default('5432'),
  DB_NAME: z.string().default('diyapp_v12'),
  DB_USER: z.string().default('postgres'),
  DB_PASSWORD: z.string().default('postgres'),
  
  // Redis
  REDIS_HOST: z.string().default('localhost'),
  REDIS_PORT: z.string().transform(Number).default('6379'),
  REDIS_PASSWORD: z.string().optional(),
  
  // RabbitMQ
  RABBITMQ_HOST: z.string().default('localhost'),
  RABBITMQ_PORT: z.string().transform(Number).default('5672'),
  RABBITMQ_USER: z.string().default('guest'),
  RABBITMQ_PASSWORD: z.string().default('guest'),
  
  // Kafka
  KAFKA_BROKERS: z.string().default('localhost:9092'),
  KAFKA_CLIENT_ID: z.string().default('diyapp-v12-core'),
  
  // JWT
  JWT_SECRET: z.string().min(32),
  JWT_EXPIRES_IN: z.string().default('24h'),
  JWT_REFRESH_SECRET: z.string().min(32),
  JWT_REFRESH_EXPIRES_IN: z.string().default('7d'),
  
  // Rate limiting
  RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS: z.string().transform(Number).default('900000'),
  RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS: z.string().transform(Number).default('100'),
  
  // External services
  EXTERNAL_API_TIMEOUT_MS: z.string().transform(Number).default('5000'),
  EXTERNAL_API_RETRY_ATTEMPTS: z.string().transform(Number).default('3'),
});

export type Config = z.infer<typeof configSchema>;

export const config: Config = configSchema.parse(process.env);

// 4. src/database/connection.ts
import { DataSource } from 'typeorm';
import { config } from '../config';
import { User } from '../core/users/entities/user.entity';
import { Task } from '../core/tasks/entities/task.entity';
import { AuditLog } from './entities/audit-log.entity';

export const AppDataSource = new DataSource({
  type: 'postgres',
  host: config.DB_HOST,
  port: config.DB_PORT,
  username: config.DB_USER,
  password: config.DB_PASSWORD,
  database: config.DB_NAME,
  synchronize: config.NODE_ENV === 'development',
  logging: config.NODE_ENV === 'development',
  entities: [User, Task, AuditLog],
  migrations: ['src/database/migrations/*.ts'],
  subscribers: [],
  poolSize: 10,
  extra: {
    connectionTimeoutMillis: 5000,
    query_timeout: 10000,
    statement_timeout: 10000,
  },
});

// 5. src/core/auth/auth.service.ts
import bcrypt from 'bcrypt';
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';
import { randomBytes } from 'crypto';
import { config } from '../../config';
import { UserService } from '../users/user.service';
import { RedisService } from '../../services/redis.service';
import { CircuitBreaker } from '../../utils/circuit-breaker';
import { logger } from '../../utils/logger';

export interface LoginCredentials {
  email: string;
  password: string;
}

export interface AuthTokens {
  accessToken: string;
  refreshToken: string;
  expiresIn: number;
}

export interface TokenPayload {
  userId: string;
  email: string;
  role: string;
  sessionId: string;
}

export class AuthService {
  private userService: UserService;
  private redisService: RedisService;
  private circuitBreaker: CircuitBreaker;
  
  constructor() {
    this.userService = new UserService();
    this.redisService = new RedisService();
    this.circuitBreaker = new CircuitBreaker({
      failureThreshold: 5,
      resetTimeout: 60000,
    });
  }
  
  async login(credentials: LoginCredentials): Promise<AuthTokens> {
    const correlationId = randomBytes(16).toString('hex');
    logger.info('Login attempt', { 
      correlationId, 
      email: this.maskEmail(credentials.email) 
    });
    
    try {
      // Validate input
      if (!credentials.email || !credentials.password) {
        throw new Error('Email and password are required');
      }
      
      // Get user with circuit breaker protection
      const user = await this.circuitBreaker.execute(
        'user-service',
        () => this.userService.findByEmail(credentials.email)
      );
      
      if (!user) {
        logger.warn('User not found', { correlationId, email: this.maskEmail(credentials.email) });
        throw new Error('Invalid credentials');
      }
      
      // Verify password
      const isValidPassword = await bcrypt.compare(credentials.password, user.passwordHash);
      if (!isValidPassword) {
        logger.warn('Invalid password', { correlationId, userId: user.id });
        throw new Error('Invalid credentials');
      }
      
      // Check if user is active
      if (!user.isActive) {
        logger.warn('Inactive user attempt', { correlationId, userId: user.id });
        throw new Error('Account is deactivated');
      }
      
      // Generate tokens
      const sessionId = randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
      const tokens = await this.generateTokens(user.id, user.email, user.role, sessionId);
      
      // Store session in Redis with TTL
      await this.redisService.set(
        `session:${sessionId}`,
        JSON.stringify({
          userId: user.id,
          email: user.email,
          role: user.role,
          lastActivity: new Date().toISOString(),
        }),
        'EX',
        7 * 24 * 60 * 60 // 7 days
      );
      
      logger.info('Login successful', { 
        correlationId, 
        userId: user.id, 
        role: user.role 
      });
      
      return tokens;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Login failed', { 
        correlationId, 
        error: error.message,
        stack: error.stack 
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }
  
  async logout(sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
    try {
      await this.redisService.del(`session:${sessionId}`);
      logger.info('Logout successful', { sessionId });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Logout failed', { sessionId, error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }
  
  async refreshToken(refreshToken: string): Promise<AuthTokens> {
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.verify(refreshToken, config.JWT_REFRESH_SECRET) as TokenPayload;
      
      // Verify session exists in Redis
      const session = await this.redisService.get(`session:${decoded.sessionId}`);
      if (!session) {
        throw new Error('Session expired');
      }
      
      // Generate new tokens
      return await this.generateTokens(
        decoded.userId,
        decoded.email,
        decoded.role,
        decoded.sessionId
      );
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Token refresh failed', { error: error.message });
      throw new Error('Invalid refresh token');
    }
  }
  
  async validateToken(token: string): Promise<TokenPayload> {
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, config.JWT_SECRET) as TokenPayload;
      
      // Verify session exists
      const session = await this.redisService.get(`session:${decoded.sessionId}`);
      if (!session) {
        throw new Error('Session expired');
      }
      
      // Update last activity
      await this.redisService.set(
        `session:${decoded.sessionId}`,
        JSON.stringify({
          ...JSON.parse(session),
          lastActivity: new Date().toISOString(),
        }),
        'EX',
        7 * 24 * 60 * 60
      );
      
      return decoded;
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Invalid token');
    }
  }
  
  private async generateTokens(
    userId: string,
    email: string,
    role: string,
    sessionId: string
  ): Promise<AuthTokens> {
    const payload: TokenPayload = {
      userId,
      email,
      role,
      sessionId,
    };
    
    const accessToken = jwt.sign(payload, config.JWT_SECRET, {
      expiresIn: config.JWT_EXPIRES_IN,
    });
    
    const refreshToken = jwt.sign(payload, config.JWT_REFRESH_SECRET, {
      expiresIn: config.JWT_REFRESH_EXPIRES_IN,
    });
    
    return {
      accessToken,
      refreshToken,
      expiresIn: 24 * 60 * 60, // 24 hours in seconds
    };
  }
  
  private maskEmail(email: string): string {
    const [local, domain] = email.split('@');
    if (local.length <= 2) return email;
    return `${local[0]}${'*'.repeat(local.length - 2)}${local.slice(-1)}@${domain}`;
  }
}

// 6. src/core/users/user.service.ts
import { AppDataSource } from '../../database/connection';
import { User } from './entities/user.entity';
import { CreateUserDto, UpdateUserDto } from './dto/user.dto';
import { logger } from '../../utils/logger';
import { randomBytes } from 'crypto';

export class UserService {
  private userRepository = AppDataSource.getRepository(User);
  
  async create(createUserDto: CreateUserDto): Promise<User> {
    const correlationId = randomBytes(16).toString('hex');
    logger.info('Creating user', { correlationId, email: this.maskEmail(createUserDto.email) });
    
    const queryRunner = AppDataSource.createQueryRunner();
    await queryRunner.connect();
    await queryRunner.startTransaction();
    
    try {
      // Check if user exists
      const existingUser = await this.userRepository.findOne({
        where: { email: createUserDto.email },
      });
      
      if (existingUser) {
        throw new Error('User with this email already exists');
      }
      
      // Create user
      const user = this.userRepository.create(createUserDto);
      const savedUser = await queryRunner.manager.save(user);
      
      await queryRunner.commitTransaction();
      
      logger.info('User created successfully', { 
        correlationId, 
        userId: savedUser.id 
      });
      
      return savedUser;
    } catch (error) {
      await queryRunner.rollbackTransaction();
      logger.error('User creation failed', { 
        correlationId, 
        error: error.message,
        stack: error.stack 
      });
      throw error;
    } finally {
      await queryRunner.release();
    }
  }
  
  async findById(id: string): Promise<User | null> {
    return await this.userRepository.findOne({
      where: { id },
      select: ['id', 'email', 'firstName', 'lastName', 'role', 'isActive', 'createdAt', 'updatedAt'],
    });
  }
  
  async findByEmail(email: string): Promise<User | null> {
    return await this.userRepository.findOne({
      where: { email },
    });
  }
  
  async update(id: string, updateUserDto: UpdateUserDto): Promise<User> {
    const correlationId = randomBytes(16).toString('hex');
    logger.info('Updating user', { correlationId, userId: id });
    
    const queryRunner = AppDataSource.createQueryRunner();
    await queryRunner.connect();
    await queryRunner.startTransaction();
    
    try {
      const user = await this.userRepository.findOne({ where: { id } });
      if (!user) {
        throw new Error('User not found');
      }
      
      // Update user
      Object.assign(user, updateUserDto);
      const updatedUser = await queryRunner.manager.save(user);
      
      await queryRunner.commitTransaction();
      
      logger.info('User updated successfully', { correlationId, userId: id });
      
      return updatedUser;
    } catch (error) {
      await queryRunner.rollbackTransaction();
      logger.error('User update failed', { 
        correlationId, 
        userId: id,
        error: error.message 
      });
      throw error;
    } finally {
      await queryRunner.release();
    }
  }
  
  async delete(id: string): Promise<void> {
    const correlationId = randomBytes(16).toString('hex');
    logger.info('Deleting user', { correlationId, userId

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]

// src/types/api.ts
export interface ApiResponse<T> {
  data: T
  message: string
  timestamp: string
}

export interface ApiError {
  code: string
  message: string
  details?: Record<string, unknown>
}

export interface PaginatedResponse<T> {
  items: T[]
  total: number
  page: number
  pageSize: number
  hasNext: boolean
  hasPrevious: boolean
}

// src/services/api.ts
import axios, { AxiosInstance, AxiosRequestConfig, AxiosResponse, AxiosError } from 'axios'
import { ApiResponse, ApiError } from '@/types/api'

class ApiService {
  private client: AxiosInstance
  private retryCount = 0
  private readonly maxRetries = 3

  constructor() {
    this.client = axios.create({
      baseURL: import.meta.env.VITE_API_BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:3001/api',
      timeout: 10000,
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      },
    })

    this.setupInterceptors()
  }

  private setupInterceptors(): void {
    // Request interceptor
    this.client.interceptors.request.use(
      (config) => {
        const token = localStorage.getItem('auth_token')
        if (token) {
          config.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${token}`
        }
        return config
      },
      (error) => {
        return Promise.reject(error)
      }
    )

    // Response interceptor with retry logic
    this.client.interceptors.response.use(
      (response) => response,
      async (error: AxiosError<ApiError>) => {
        const originalRequest = error.config as AxiosRequestConfig & { _retry?: boolean }
        
        // Retry on network errors or 5xx status codes
        if (
          !originalRequest._retry &&
          this.retryCount < this.maxRetries &&
          (!error.response || (error.response.status >= 500 && error.response.status < 600))
        ) {
          this.retryCount++
          originalRequest._retry = true
          
          // Exponential backoff
          const delay = Math.pow(2, this.retryCount) * 1000
          await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay))
          
          return this.client(originalRequest)
        }
        
        this.retryCount = 0
        return Promise.reject(error)
      }
    )
  }

  async get<T>(url: string, config?: AxiosRequestConfig): Promise<ApiResponse<T>> {
    try {
      const response: AxiosResponse<ApiResponse<T>> = await this.client.get(url, config)
      return response.data
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleError(error)
      throw error
    }
  }

  async post<T>(url: string, data?: unknown, config?: AxiosRequestConfig): Promise<ApiResponse<T>> {
    try {
      const response: AxiosResponse<ApiResponse<T>> = await this.client.post(url, data, config)
      return response.data
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleError(error)
      throw error
    }
  }

  async put<T>(url: string, data?: unknown, config?: AxiosRequestConfig): Promise<ApiResponse<T>> {
    try {
      const response: AxiosResponse<ApiResponse<T>> = await this.client.put(url, data, config)
      return response.data
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleError(error)
      throw error
    }
  }

  async delete<T>(url: string, config?: AxiosRequestConfig): Promise<ApiResponse<T>> {
    try {
      const response: AxiosResponse<ApiResponse<T>> = await this.client.delete(url, config)
      return response.data
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleError(error)
      throw error
    }
  }

  private handleError(error: unknown): void {
    if (axios.isAxiosError(error)) {
      const apiError = error.response?.data as ApiError
      console.error('API Error:', {
        code: apiError?.code || 'UNKNOWN_ERROR',
        message: apiError?.message || error.message,
        status: error.response?.status,
        url: error.config?.url,
      })
    } else {
      console.error('Unexpected error:', error)
    }
  }
}

export const apiService = new ApiService()

// src/services/dashboardService.ts
import { apiService } from './api'
import { DashboardStats, ChartDataPoint, KanbanColumn } from '@/types/dashboard'
import { ApiResponse, PaginatedResponse } from '@/types/api'

export class DashboardService {
  async getDashboardStats(): Promise<DashboardStats> {
    try {
      const response = await apiService.get<DashboardStats>('/dashboard/stats')
      return response.data
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to fetch dashboard stats:', error)
      throw error
    }
  }

  async getChartData(timeRange: 'day' | 'week' | 'month' | 'year'): Promise<ChartDataPoint[]> {
    try {
      const response = await apiService.get<ChartDataPoint[]>(`/dashboard/chart?range=${timeRange}`)
      return response.data
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to fetch chart data:', error)
      throw error
    }
  }

  async getKanbanBoard(): Promise<KanbanColumn[]> {
    try {
      const response = await apiService.get<KanbanColumn[]>('/dashboard/kanban')
      return response.data
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to fetch kanban board:', error)
      throw error
    }
  }

  async updateTaskStatus(taskId: string, status: string): Promise<void> {
    try {
      await apiService.put(`/tasks/${taskId}/status`, { status })
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to update task status:', error)
      throw error
    }
  }

  async createTask(task: Omit<KanbanColumn

### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
```sql
-- ============================================
-- DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core
-- Database Schema & ETL Pipelines
-- Senior Data Engineer Implementation
-- ============================================

-- ============================================
-- 1. DATABASE SCHEMA (PostgreSQL 15+)
-- ============================================

-- ====================
-- 1.1 Core Tables (V12)
-- ====================

-- Users table with GDPR compliance
CREATE TABLE users (
    user_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    external_id VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE, -- For backward compatibility with V11
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    username VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE,
    hashed_password VARCHAR(255),
    full_name VARCHAR(255),
    avatar_url TEXT,
    timezone VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'UTC',
    locale VARCHAR(10) DEFAULT 'en-US',
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    is_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    verification_token VARCHAR(255),
    reset_token VARCHAR(255),
    last_login_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    deleted_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    gdpr_consent_given_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    gdpr_data_retention_until TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    -- Indexes for performance
    INDEX idx_users_email ON users(email),
    INDEX idx_users_created_at ON users(created_at),
    INDEX idx_users_deleted_at ON users(deleted_at) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL
);

-- Organizations/Teams
CREATE TABLE organizations (
    org_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    slug VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    logo_url TEXT,
    website_url TEXT,
    industry VARCHAR(100),
    size_range VARCHAR(50), -- '1-10', '11-50', '51-200', '201-500', '501-1000', '1000+'
    billing_tier VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'free',
    subscription_status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'active',
    trial_ends_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    INDEX idx_orgs_slug ON organizations(slug),
    INDEX idx_orgs_billing_tier ON organizations(billing_tier)
);

-- Organization members (many-to-many)
CREATE TABLE organization_members (
    org_member_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    org_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES organizations(org_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    role VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'member', -- 'owner', 'admin', 'member', 'guest'
    permissions JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    joined_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    invited_by UUID REFERENCES users(user_id),
    invitation_token VARCHAR(255),
    invitation_status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'active', -- 'pending', 'active', 'revoked'
    
    UNIQUE(org_id, user_id),
    INDEX idx_org_members_user ON organization_members(user_id),
    INDEX idx_org_members_org ON organization_members(org_id)
);

-- Projects
CREATE TABLE projects (
    project_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    org_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES organizations(org_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    slug VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    icon VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT '📁',
    color VARCHAR(7) DEFAULT '#3B82F6',
    is_public BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    settings JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    created_by UUID REFERENCES users(user_id),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    archived_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    UNIQUE(org_id, slug),
    INDEX idx_projects_org ON projects(org_id),
    INDEX idx_projects_created_at ON projects(created_at)
);

-- Tasks
CREATE TABLE tasks (
    task_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES projects(project_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    external_task_id VARCHAR(255), -- For V11 migration
    title VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'todo', -- 'todo', 'in_progress', 'review', 'done', 'blocked'
    priority VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'medium', -- 'low', 'medium', 'high', 'critical'
    estimate_minutes INTEGER,
    actual_minutes INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    due_date TIMESTAMPTZ,
    completed_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    assigned_to UUID REFERENCES users(user_id),
    created_by UUID REFERENCES users(user_id),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    deleted_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    -- Indexes for common queries
    INDEX idx_tasks_project_status ON tasks(project_id, status),
    INDEX idx_tasks_assigned_to ON tasks(assigned_to),
    INDEX idx_tasks_due_date ON tasks(due_date),
    INDEX idx_tasks_created_at ON tasks(created_at)
);

-- Task comments/discussions
CREATE TABLE task_comments (
    comment_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    task_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tasks(task_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(user_id),
    parent_comment_id UUID REFERENCES task_comments(comment_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    content TEXT NOT NULL,
    mentions JSONB DEFAULT '[]', -- Array of mentioned user IDs
    attachments JSONB DEFAULT '[]', -- Array of attachment metadata
    is_pinned BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    deleted_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    INDEX idx_comments_task ON task_comments(task_id),
    INDEX idx_comments_user ON task_comments(user_id),
    INDEX idx_comments_created_at ON task_comments(created_at)
);

-- ====================
-- 1.2 Analytics Tables
-- ====================

-- User activity events (raw events for analytics)
CREATE TABLE user_events_raw (
    event_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    event_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, -- 'user_login', 'task_created', 'task_completed', etc.
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(user_id),
    org_id UUID REFERENCES organizations(org_id),
    project_id UUID REFERENCES projects(project_id),
    task_id UUID REFERENCES tasks(task_id),
    session_id VARCHAR(255),
    user_agent TEXT,
    ip_address INET,
    device_type VARCHAR(50), -- 'desktop', 'mobile', 'tablet'
    browser VARCHAR(100),
    os VARCHAR(100),
    country_code CHAR(2),
    event_data JSONB DEFAULT '{}', -- Additional event-specific data
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Partition by month for performance
    PARTITION BY RANGE (created_at)
);

-- Create monthly partitions for events
CREATE TABLE user_events_raw_2024_01 PARTITION OF user_events_raw
    FOR VALUES FROM ('2024-01-01') TO ('2024-02-01');

CREATE TABLE user_events_raw_2024_02 PARTITION OF user_events_raw
    FOR VALUES FROM ('2024-02-01') TO ('2024-03-01');

-- Indexes for event queries
CREATE INDEX idx_events_user_date ON user_events_raw(user_id, created_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_events_type_date ON user_events_raw(event_type, created_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_events_org_date ON user_events_raw(org_id, created_at);

-- ====================
-- 1.3 LLM/AI Analytics Tables
-- ====================

-- LLM API calls tracking
CREATE TABLE llm_calls (
    call_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- 'openai', 'anthropic', 'google', 'azure'
    model VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, -- 'gpt-4', 'claude-3-opus', etc.
    endpoint VARCHAR(100), -- 'chat/completions', 'embeddings', etc.
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(user_id),
    org_id UUID REFERENCES organizations(org_id),
    project_id UUID REFERENCES projects(project_id),
    task_id UUID REFERENCES tasks(task_id),
    input_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    output_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    total_tokens INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS (input_tokens + output_tokens) STORED,
    cost_usd DECIMAL(10,6), -- Calculated cost
    latency_ms INTEGER, -- Response time in milliseconds
    success BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    error_message TEXT,
    request_metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    response_metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    INDEX idx_llm_calls_user_date ON llm_calls(user_id, created_at),
    INDEX idx_llm_calls_org_date ON llm_calls(org_id, created_at),
    INDEX idx_llm_calls_provider_model ON llm_calls(provider, model)
);

-- ====================
-- 1.4 Audit Tables
-- ====================

-- Data changes audit trail
CREATE TABLE audit_logs (
    audit_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    table_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    record_id UUID NOT NULL,
    operation VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL, -- 'INSERT', 'UPDATE', 'DELETE'
    old_values JSONB,
    new_values JSONB,
    changed_by UUID REFERENCES users(user_id),
    changed_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    ip_address INET,
    user_agent TEXT,
    
    INDEX idx_audit_table_record ON audit_logs(table_name, record_id),
    INDEX idx_audit_changed_at ON audit_logs(changed_at)
);

-- ============================================
-- 2. ETL PIPELINES (dbt models)
-- ============================================

-- models/sources.yml
-- sources:
--   - name: diyapp_raw
--     database: diyapp_production
--     schema: public
--     tables:
--       - name: users
--       - name: organizations
