-- models/staging/stg_users.sql
WITH source AS (
    SELECT
        user_id,
        external_id,
        email,
        username,
        full_name,
        avatar_url,
        timezone,
        locale,
        is_active,
        is_verified,
        last_login_at,
        created_at,
        updated_at,
        deleted_at,
        gdpr_consent_given_at,
        gdpr_data_retention_until
    FROM {{ source('diyapp_raw', 'users') }}
),

cleaned AS (
    SELECT
        user_id,
        external_id,
        -- Email validation and cleaning
        LOWER(TRIM(email)) AS email,
        -- Username cleaning
        CASE 
            WHEN username IS NOT NULL THEN LOWER(TRIM(username))
            ELSE NULL
        END AS username,
        -- Name cleaning
        INITCAP(TRIM(full_name)) AS full_name,
        avatar_url,
        COALESCE(timezone, 'UTC') AS timezone,
        COALESCE(locale, 'en-US') AS locale,
        COALESCE(is_active, true) AS is_active,
        COALESCE(is_verified, false) AS is_verified,
        last_login_at,
        created_at,
        updated_at,
        deleted_at,
        gdpr_consent_given_at,
        gdpr_data_retention_until,
        -- Data quality flags
        CASE 
            WHEN email ~ '^[A-Za-z0-9._%+-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.-]+\.[A-Za-z]{2,}$' THEN true
            ELSE false
        END AS is_valid_email,
        CASE 
            WHEN deleted_at IS NOT NULL THEN 'deleted'
            WHEN is_active = false THEN 'inactive'
            WHEN is_verified = false THEN 'unverified'
            ELSE 'active'
        END AS user_status
    FROM source
)

SELECT * FROM cleaned

-- models/staging/stg_organizations.sql
WITH source AS (
    SELECT
        org_id,
        name,
        slug,
        description,
        logo_url,
        website_url,
        industry,
        size_range,
        billing_tier,
        subscription_status,
        trial_ends_at,
        created_at,
        updated_at
    FROM {{ source('diyapp_raw', 'organizations') }}
),

cleaned AS (
    SELECT
        org_id,
        TRIM(name) AS name,
        LOWER(TRIM(slug)) AS slug,
        description,
        logo_url,
        website_url,
        industry,
        size_range,
        COALESCE(billing_tier, 'free') AS billing_tier,
        COALESCE(subscription_status, 'active') AS subscription_status,
        trial_ends_at,
        created_at,
        updated_at,
        -- Business logic flags
        CASE 
            WHEN billing_tier IN ('enterprise', 'business') THEN 'paid'
            WHEN billing_tier = 'pro' THEN 'pro'
            ELSE 'free'
        END AS billing_category,
        CASE 
            WHEN trial_ends_at IS NOT NULL AND trial_ends_at > CURRENT_TIMESTAMP 
            THEN 'in_trial'
            ELSE 'not_in_trial'
        END AS trial_status
    FROM source
)

SELECT * FROM cleaned

-- models/staging/stg_llm_calls.sql
WITH source AS (
    SELECT
        call_id,
        provider,
        model,
        endpoint,
        user_id,
        org_id,
        project_id,
        task_id,
        input_tokens,
        output_tokens,
        total_tokens,
        cost_usd,
        latency_ms,
        success,
        error_message,
        request_metadata,
        response_metadata,
        created_at
    FROM {{ source('diyapp_raw', 'llm_calls') }}
),

cleaned AS (
    SELECT
        call_id,
        LOWER(provider) AS provider,
        model,
        endpoint,
        user_id,
        org_id,
        project_id,
        task_id,
        -- Handle null tokens
        COALESCE(input_tokens, 0) AS input_tokens,
        COALESCE(output_tokens, 0) AS output_tokens,
        COALESCE(total_tokens, COALESCE(input_tokens, 0) + COALESCE(output_tokens, 0)) AS total_tokens,
        -- Calculate cost if not provided
        COALESCE(cost_usd,
            CASE 
                WHEN provider = 'openai' AND model LIKE 'gpt-4%' THEN (input_tokens * 0.00003 + output_tokens * 0.00006)
                WHEN provider = 'openai' AND model LIKE 'gpt-3.5%' THEN (input_tokens * 0.0000015 + output_tokens * 0.000002)
                WHEN provider = 'anthropic' AND model LIKE 'claude-3%' THEN (input_tokens * 0.000015 + output_tokens * 0.000075)
                ELSE 0
            END
        ) AS cost_usd,
        latency_ms,
        COALESCE(success, true) AS success,
        error_message,
        request_metadata,
        response_metadata,
        created_at,
        -- Cost categorization
        CASE 
            WHEN cost_usd > 1 THEN 'high_cost'
            WHEN cost_usd > 0.1 THEN 'medium_cost'
            ELSE 'low_cost'
        END AS cost_category
    FROM source
)

SELECT * FROM cleaned

-- models/marts/mart_product/daily_active_users.sql
WITH daily_events AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(created_at) AS event_date,
        user_id,
        org_id,
        COUNT(DISTINCT event_type) AS distinct_event_types,
        COUNT(*) AS total_events
    FROM {{ ref('stg_user_events') }}
    WHERE created_at >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '30 days'
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3
),

user_sessions AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(created_at) AS session_date,
        user_id,
        COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) AS daily_sessions,
        MIN(created_at) AS first_event_time,
        MAX(created_at) AS last_event_time
    FROM {{ ref('stg_user_events') }}
    WHERE created_at >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '30 days'
    GROUP BY 1, 2
)

SELECT
    de.event_date,
    de.user_id,
    de.org_id,
    u.username,
    u.email,
    o.name AS org_name,
    o.billing_tier,
    de.distinct_event_types,
    de.total_events,
    us.daily_sessions,
    EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (us.last_event_time - us.first_event_time)) / 3600 AS session_duration_hours,
    -- Engagement score
    CASE 
        WHEN de.total_events > 50 THEN 'high'
        WHEN de.total_events > 10 THEN 'medium'
        ELSE 'low'
    END AS engagement_level
FROM daily_events de
LEFT JOIN {{ ref('stg_users') }} u ON de.user_id = u.user_id
LEFT JOIN {{ ref('stg_organizations') }} o ON de.org_id = o.org_id
LEFT JOIN user_sessions us ON de.event_date = us.session_date AND de.user_id = us.user_id
WHERE u.deleted_at IS NULL
  AND u.is_active = true

-- models/marts/mart_ai/llm_cost_by_feature.sql
WITH llm_calls_enriched AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(lc.created_at) AS call_date,
        lc.provider,
        lc.model,
        lc.user_id,
        lc.org_id,
        lc.project_id,
        lc.task_id,
        ue.event_type,
        ue.event_data->>'feature' AS feature_name,
        lc.input_tokens,
        lc.output_tokens,
        lc.total_tokens,
        lc.cost_usd

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Arquitetura de Microsserviços

```yaml
# docker-compose.yml - Orquestração de Microsserviços
version: '3.8'

services:
  # API Gateway
  api-gateway:
    build: ./services/api-gateway
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - LOG_LEVEL=info
      - JAEGER_AGENT_HOST=jaeger
      - REDIS_HOST=redis
    depends_on:
      - auth-service
      - user-service
      - content-service
      - redis
      - jaeger
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
    deploy:
      resources:
        limits:
          memory: 512M
        reservations:
          memory: 256M

  # Serviço de Autenticação
  auth-service:
    build: ./services/auth
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - JWT_SECRET=${JWT_SECRET}
      - REDIS_HOST=redis
      - POSTGRES_HOST=postgres
      - POSTGRES_DB=auth_db
      - POSTGRES_USER=${DB_USER}
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${DB_PASSWORD}
    depends_on:
      - postgres
      - redis
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3001/health"]
      interval: 30s

  # Serviço de Usuários
  user-service:
    build: ./services/users
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - POSTGRES_HOST=postgres
      - POSTGRES_DB=users_db
      - REDIS_HOST=redis
      - ELASTICSEARCH_HOST=elasticsearch
    depends_on:
      - postgres
      - redis
      - elasticsearch
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Serviço de Conteúdo
  content-service:
    build: ./services/content
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - POSTGRES_HOST=postgres
      - POSTGRES_DB=content_db
      - MINIO_HOST=minio
      - MINIO_ACCESS_KEY=${MINIO_ACCESS_KEY}
      - MINIO_SECRET_KEY=${MINIO_SECRET_KEY}
    depends_on:
      - postgres
      - minio
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Banco de Dados PostgreSQL
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_MULTIPLE_DATABASES=auth_db,users_db,content_db
      - POSTGRES_USER=${DB_USER}
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./scripts/init-databases.sh:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init-databases.sh
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U ${DB_USER}"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Redis para Cache e Sessões
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s

  # MinIO para Armazenamento de Arquivos
  minio:
    image: minio/minio
    command: server /data --console-address ":9001"
    environment:
      - MINIO_ROOT_USER=${MINIO_ROOT_USER}
      - MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD=${MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - minio_data:/data
    ports:
      - "9000:9000"
      - "9001:9001"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Elasticsearch para Busca e Logs
  elasticsearch:
    image: elasticsearch:8.11.0
    environment:
      - discovery.type=single-node
      - xpack.security.enabled=false
      - "ES_JAVA_OPTS=-Xms512m -Xmx512m"
    volumes:
      - elasticsearch_data:/usr/share/elasticsearch/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:9200"]
      interval: 30s

  # Jaeger para Distributed Tracing
  jaeger:
    image: jaegertracing/all-in-one:1.48
    ports:
      - "16686:16686"
      - "6831:6831/udp"
    environment:
      - COLLECTOR_OTLP_ENABLED=true
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Prometheus para Métricas
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    volumes:
      - ./monitoring/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
      - prometheus_data:/prometheus
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
      - '--web.console.libraries=/etc/prometheus/console_libraries'
      - '--web.console.templates=/etc/prometheus/consoles'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=200h'
      - '--web.enable-lifecycle'
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Grafana para Dashboards
  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=${GRAFANA_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./monitoring/dashboards:/etc/grafana/provisioning/dashboards
      - ./monitoring/datasources:/etc/grafana/provisioning/datasources
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    depends_on:
      - prometheus
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

networks:
  diyapp-network:
    driver: bridge
    ipam:
      config:
        - subnet: 172.20.0.0/16

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  redis_data:
  minio_data:
  elasticsearch_data:
  prometheus_data:
  grafana_data:
```

```bash
# scripts/init-databases.sh
#!/bin/bash

set -e
set -u

function create_user_and_database() {
    local database=$1
    echo "Creating database '$database'"
    psql -v ON_ERROR_STOP=1 --username "$POSTGRES_USER" <<-EOSQL
        CREATE DATABASE $database;
        GRANT ALL PRIVILEGES ON DATABASE $database TO $POSTGRES_USER;
EOSQL
}

if [ -n "$POSTGRES_MULTIPLE_DATABASES" ]; then
    echo "Multiple database creation requested: $POSTGRES_MULTIPLE_DATABASES"
    for db in $(echo $POSTGRES_MULTIPLE_DATABASES | tr ',' ' '); do
        create_user_and_database $db
    done
    echo "Multiple databases created"
fi
```

```javascript
// services/api-gateway/src/index.js - API Gateway com Circuit Breaker
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const { createProxyMiddleware } = require('http-proxy-middleware');
const CircuitBreaker = require('opossum');
const winston = require('winston');
const { JaegerTracer, initTracer } = require('jaeger-client');
const promClient = require('prom-client');

// Configuração de Logs
const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console(),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/api-gateway.log' })
  ]
});

// Métricas Prometheus
const collectDefaultMetrics = promClient.collectDefaultMetrics;
collectDefaultMetrics({ timeout: 5000 });

const requestCounter = new promClient.Counter({
  name: 'http_requests_total',
  help: 'Total HTTP requests',
  labelNames: ['method', 'route', 'status_code']
});

const requestDuration = new promClient.Histogram({
  name: 'http_request_duration_seconds',
  help: 'HTTP request duration in seconds',
  labelNames: ['method', 'route', 'status_code'],
  buckets: [0.1, 0.5, 1, 2, 5]
});

// Configuração Jaeger
const config = {
  serviceName: 'api-gateway',
  sampler: {
    type: 'const',
    param: 1
  },
  reporter: {
    logSpans: true,
    agentHost: process.env.JAEGER_AGENT_HOST || 'localhost'
  }
};

const options = {};
const tracer = initTracer(config, options);

const app = express();

// Middlewares de Segurança
app.use(helmet());
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS.split(',') : '*',
  credentials: true
}));

// Rate Limiting
const limiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
  max: 100, // limite por IP
  message: 'Too many requests from this IP'
});
app.use('/api/', limiter);

// Health Check
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
  res.status(200).json({
    status: 'healthy',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    service: 'api-gateway',
    version: process.env.npm_package_version || '1.0.0'
  });
});

// Métricas Endpoint
app.get('/metrics', async (req, res) => {
  res.set('Content-Type', promClient.register.contentType);
  res.end(await promClient.register.metrics());
});

// Circuit Breakers por serviço
const circuitBreakers = {
  auth: new CircuitBreaker(async (req, res, next) => {
    // Proxy para auth-service
    return createProxyMiddleware({
      target: 'http://auth-service:3001',
      changeOrigin: true,
      pathRewrite: { '^/api/auth': '' }
    })(req, res, next);
  }, {
    timeout: 5000,
    errorThresholdPercentage: 50,
    resetTimeout: 30000
  }),

  users: new CircuitBreaker(async (req, res, next) => {
    return createProxyMiddleware({
      target: 'http://user-service:3002',
      changeOrigin: true,
      pathRewrite: { '^/api/users': '' }
    })(req, res, next);
  }, {
    timeout: 3000,
    errorThresholdPercentage: 40,
    resetTimeout: 20000
  }),

  content: new CircuitBreaker(async (req, res, next) => {
    return createProxyMiddleware({
      target: 'http://content-service:3003',
      changeOrigin: true,
      pathRewrite: { '^/api/content': '' }
    })(req, res, next);
  }, {
    timeout: 10000,
    errorThresholdPercentage: 30,
    resetTimeout: 60000
  })
};

// Middleware de Tracing
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  const span = tracer.startSpan(req.path);
  span.setTag('http.method', req.method);
  span.setTag('http.url', req.url);
  
  req.traceSpan = span;
  
  res.on('finish', () => {
    span.setTag('http.status_code', res.statusCode);
    span.finish();
  });
  
  next();
});

// Middleware de Métricas
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  const start = Date.now();
  
  res.on('finish', () => {
    const duration = (Date.now() - start) / 1000;
    requestCounter.inc({
      method: req.method,
      route: req.route?.path || req.path,
      status_code: res.statusCode
    });
    
    requestDuration.observe({
      method: req.method,
      route: req.route?.path || req.path,
      status_code: res.statusCode
    }, duration);
    
    logger.info({
      method: req.method,
      url: req.url,
      status: res.statusCode,
      duration: `${duration}s`,
      userAgent: req.get('User-Agent'),
      ip: req.ip
    });
  });
  
  next();
});

// Rotas com Circuit Breaker
app.use('/api/auth', async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    await circuitBreakers.auth.fire(req, res, next);
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Auth service circuit breaker open', { error: error.message });
    res.status(503).json({
      error: 'Authentication service temporarily unavailable',
      retryAfter: 30
    });
  }
});

app.use('/api/users', async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    await circuitBreakers.users.fire(req, res, next);
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Users service circuit breaker open', { error: error.message });
    res.status(503).json({
      error: 'Users service temporarily unavailable',
      retryAfter: 20
    });
  }
});

app.use('/api/content', async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    await circuitBreakers.content.fire(req, res, next);
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Content service circuit breaker open', { error: error.message });
    res.status(503).json({
      error: 'Content service temporarily unavailable',
      retryAfter: 60
    });
  }
});

// Error Handling
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  logger.error('Unhandled error', {
    error: err.message,
    stack: err.stack,
    url: req.url,
    method: req.method
  });
  
  if (req.traceSpan) {
    req.traceSpan.setTag('error', true);
    req.traceSpan.log({ 'error.message': err.message });
  }
  
  res.status(500).json({
    error: 'Internal server error',
    requestId: req.traceSpan?.context().traceIdStr
  });
});

const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;
app.listen(PORT, () => {
  logger.info(`API Gateway running on port ${PORT}`);
});

module.exports = app;
```

```javascript
// services/auth/src/index.js - Serviço de Autenticação
const express = require('express');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const redis = require('redis');
const winston = require('winston');
const promClient = require('prom-client');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

// Configuração
const app = express();
app.use(express.json());

// Logger
const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console(),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/auth-service.log' })
  ]
});

// Métricas
const authRequests = new promClient.Counter({
  name: 'auth_requests_total',
  help: 'Total authentication requests',
  labelNames: ['type', 'status']
});

const authDuration = new promClient.Histogram({
  name: 'auth_request_duration_seconds',
  help: 'Authentication request duration',
  labelNames: ['type'],
  buckets: [0.1, 0.5, 1, 2]
});

// Database Pool
const pool = new Pool({
  host: process.env.POSTGRES_HOST || 'localhost',
  database: process.env.POSTGRES_DB || 'auth_db',
  user: process.env.POSTGRES_USER || 'postgres',
  password: process.env.POSTGRES_PASSWORD || 'postgres',
  port: 5432,
  max: 20,
  idleTimeoutMillis: 30000,
  connectionTimeoutMillis: 2000
});

// Redis Client
const redisClient = redis.createClient({
  url: `redis://${process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost'}:6379`
});

redisClient.on('error', (err) => logger.error('Redis Client Error', err));

// Health Check
app.get('/health', async (req, res) => {
  const checks = {
    database: false,
    redis: false,
    service: true
  };

  try {
    await pool.query('SELECT 1');
    checks.database = true;
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error('Database health check failed', err);
  }

  try {
    await redisClient.ping();
    checks.redis = true;
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error('Redis health check failed', err);
  }

  const healthy = Object.values(checks).every(v => v);
  
  res.status(healthy ? 200 : 503).json({
    status: healthy ? 'healthy' : 'unhealthy',
    checks,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
  });
});

// Registro de Usuário
app.post('/register', async (req, res) => {
  const end = authDuration.startTimer({ type: 'register' });
  
  try {
    const { email, password, name } = req.body;
    
    if (!email || !password || !name) {
      authRequests.inc({ type: 'register', status: 'validation_error' });
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing required fields' });
    }

    // Verificar

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Sistema de Design

Vou criar um sistema de design completo com tokens, componentes atômicos e protótipos interativos para o DIYAPP V12.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-design-system/
├── index.html
├── design-system/
│   ├── tokens/
│   │   ├── colors.css
│   │   ├── typography.css
│   │   ├── spacing.css
│   │   ├── shadows.css
│   │   └── index.css
│   ├── components/
│   │   ├── atoms/
│   │   ├── molecules/
│   │   ├── organisms/
│   │   └── templates/
│   └── prototypes/
│       ├── auth-flow/
│       ├── dashboard/
│       └── ai-workflow/
├── src/
│   ├── styles/
│   │   └── main.css
│   ├── scripts/
│   │   └── prototype.js
│   └── utils/
│       └── design-tokens.js
└── README.md
```

### design-system/tokens/typography.css
```css
:root {
  /* Font Families */
  --font-family-sans: 'Inter', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, sans-serif;
  --font-family-mono: 'JetBrains Mono', 'SF Mono', Monaco, 'Cascadia Mono', monospace;
  
  /* Font Sizes - Scale */
  --font-size-xs: 0.75rem;     /* 12px */
  --font-size-sm: 0.875rem;    /* 14px */
  --font-size-base: 1rem;      /* 16px */
  --font-size-lg: 1.125rem;    /* 18px */
  --font-size-xl: 1.25rem;     /* 20px */
  --font-size-2xl: 1.5rem;     /* 24px */
  --font-size-3xl: 1.875rem;   /* 30px */
  --font-size-4xl: 2.25rem;    /* 36px */
  --font-size-5xl: 3rem;       /* 48px */
  --font-size-6xl: 3.75rem;    /* 60px */
  
  /* Font Weights */
  --font-weight-light: 300;
  --font-weight-normal: 400;
  --font-weight-medium: 500;
  --font-weight-semibold: 600;
  --font-weight-bold: 700;
  
  /* Line Heights */
  --line-height-tight: 1.25;
  --line-height-normal: 1.5;
  --line-height-relaxed: 1.75;
  --line-height-loose: 2;
  
  /* Letter Spacing */
  --letter-spacing-tighter: -0.05em;
  --letter-spacing-tight: -0.025em;
  --letter-spacing-normal: 0;
  --letter-spacing-wide: 0.025em;

// src/config/env.ts
import dotenv from 'dotenv';
import { z } from 'zod';

dotenv.config();

const envSchema = z.object({
  NODE_ENV: z.enum(['development', 'test', 'production']).default('development'),
  PORT: z.string().transform(Number).default('3000'),
  DATABASE_URL: z.string().min(1),
  JWT_SECRET: z.string().min(32),
  JWT_EXPIRES_IN: z.string().default('24h'),
  RABBITMQ_URL: z.string().optional(),
  KAFKA_BROKERS: z.string().optional(),
  REDIS_URL: z.string().optional(),
  RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS: z.string().transform(Number).default('900000'),
  RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS: z.string().transform(Number).default('100'),
  LOG_LEVEL: z.enum(['error', 'warn', 'info', 'debug']).default('info'),
  API_VERSION: z.string().default('v1')
});

export type EnvConfig = z.infer<typeof envSchema>;

let env: EnvConfig;

try {
  env = envSchema.parse(process.env);
} catch (error) {
  console.error('❌ Invalid environment variables:', error.errors);
  process.exit(1);
}

export default env;

// 4. CONFIGURAÇÃO DE LOGGING
// src/utils/logger.ts
import winston from 'winston';
import { AsyncLocalStorage } from 'async_hooks';

const asyncLocalStorage = new AsyncLocalStorage<Map<string, string>>();

export const getCorrelationId = (): string => {
  const store = asyncLocalStorage.getStore();
  return store?.get('correlationId') || 'unknown';
};

export const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.json(),
    winston.format((info) => {
      const correlationId = getCorrelationId();
      return {
        ...info,
        correlation_id: correlationId,
        service: 'diyapp-core',
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      };
    })()
  ),
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console(),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/error.log', level: 'error' }),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/combined.log' })
  ]
});

export const withCorrelationId = <T extends (...args: any[]) => any>(
  fn: T,
  correlationId: string = crypto.randomUUID()
): ReturnType<T> => {
  const store = new Map<string, string>();
  store.set('correlationId', correlationId);
  return asyncLocalStorage.run(store, fn);
};

// 6. ENTIDADES DO BANCO DE DADOS
// src/database/entities/user.entity.ts
import { Entity, PrimaryGeneratedColumn, Column, CreateDateColumn, UpdateDateColumn, Index } from 'typeorm';

@Entity('users')
export class User {
  @PrimaryGeneratedColumn('uuid')
  id!: string;

  @Column({ unique: true })
  @Index()
  email!: string;

  @Column()
  name!: string;

  @Column()
  passwordHash!: string;

  @Column({ default: true })
  isActive!: boolean;

  @CreateDateColumn()
  createdAt!: Date;

  @UpdateDateColumn()
  updatedAt!: Date;

  // Métodos de negócio
  static async hashPassword(password: string): Promise<string> {
    const bcrypt = await import('bcrypt');
    return bcrypt.hash(password, 10);
  }

  async validatePassword(password: string): Promise<boolean> {
    const bcrypt = await import('bcrypt');
    return bcrypt.compare(password, this.passwordHash);
  }
}

// 7. REPOSITÓRIO DE USUÁRIOS
// src/core/users/user.repository.ts
import { Repository } from 'typeorm';
import { AppDataSource } from '../../database/data-source';
import { User } from '../../database/entities/user.entity';
import { logger } from '../../utils/logger';

export class UserRepository {
  private repository: Repository<User>;

  constructor() {
    this.repository = AppDataSource.getRepository(User);
  }

  async create(userData: Partial<User>): Promise<User> {
    const queryRunner = AppDataSource.createQueryRunner();
    await queryRunner.connect();
    await queryRunner.startTransaction();

    try {
      const user = this.repository.create(userData);
      const savedUser = await queryRunner.manager.save(user);
      
      await queryRunner.commitTransaction();
      
      logger.info('User created successfully', { userId: savedUser.id });
      return savedUser;
    } catch (error) {
      await queryRunner.rollbackTransaction();
      
      if (error.code === '23505') { // Unique violation
        throw new Error('USER_ALREADY_EXISTS');
      }
      
      logger.error('Failed to create user', { error, correlationId: logger.getCorrelationId() });
      throw error;
    } finally {
      await queryRunner.release();
    }
  }

  async findByEmail(email: string): Promise<User | null> {
    try {
      return await this.repository.findOne({ where: { email } });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to find user by email', { 
        email: email.replace(/@.*/, '@***'), // Mask email in logs
        error,
        correlationId: logger.getCorrelationId()
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async findById(id: string): Promise<User | null> {
    try {
      return await this.repository.findOne({ where: { id } });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to find user by ID', { 
        userId: id,
        error,
        correlationId: logger.getCorrelationId()
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async update(id: string, updates: Partial<User>): Promise<User | null> {
    const queryRunner = AppDataSource.createQueryRunner();
    await queryRunner.connect();
    await queryRunner.startTransaction();

    try {
      await queryRunner.manager.update(User, { id }, updates);
      const updatedUser = await queryRunner.manager.findOne(User, { where: { id } });
      
      await queryRunner.commitTransaction();
      
      if (updatedUser) {
        logger.info('User updated successfully', { userId: id });
      }
      
      return updatedUser;
    } catch (error) {
      await queryRunner.rollbackTransaction();
      logger.error('Failed to update user', { userId: id, error, correlationId: logger.getCorrelationId() });
      throw error;
    } finally {
      await queryRunner.release();
    }
  }
}

// 8. SERVICE DE AUTENTICAÇÃO
// src/core/auth/auth.service.ts
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';
import { UserRepository } from '../users/user.repository';
import { User } from '../../database/entities/user.entity';
import env from '../../config/env';
import { logger } from '../../utils/logger';
import { CircuitBreaker } from '../../utils/circuit-breaker';

export interface RegisterInput {
  email: string;
  password: string;
  name: string;
}

export interface LoginInput {
  email: string;
  password: string;
}

export interface AuthResponse {
  token: string;
  user: {
    id: string;
    email: string;
    name: string;
    createdAt: Date;
    updatedAt: Date;
  };
}

export class AuthService {
  private userRepository: UserRepository;
  private circuitBreaker: CircuitBreaker;

  constructor() {
    this.userRepository = new UserRepository();
    this.circuitBreaker = new CircuitBreaker({
      failureThreshold: 5,
      resetTimeout: 60000,
      timeout: 5000
    });
  }

  async register(input: RegisterInput): Promise<AuthResponse> {
    // Validação de negócio
    if (!this.isValidEmail(input.email)) {
      throw new Error('INVALID_EMAIL');
    }

    if (!this.isStrongPassword(input.password)) {
      throw new Error('WEAK_PASSWORD');
    }

    try {
      // Usa circuit breaker para operações de banco
      const user = await this.circuitBreaker.execute(async () => {
        const existingUser = await this.userRepository.findByEmail(input.email);
        if (existingUser) {
          throw new Error('USER_ALREADY_EXISTS');
        }

        const passwordHash = await User.hashPassword(input.password);
        return this.userRepository.create({
          email: input.email,
          name: input.name,
          passwordHash
        });
      });

      const token = this.generateToken(user);
      
      logger.info('User registered successfully', { 
        userId: user.id,
        email: user.email.replace(/@.*/, '@***')
      });

      return {
        token,
        user: {
          id: user.id,
          email: user.email,
          name: user.name,
          createdAt: user.createdAt,
          updatedAt: user.updatedAt
        }
      };
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Registration failed', { 
        error: error.message,
        email: input.email.replace(/@.*/, '@***'),
        correlationId: logger.getCorrelationId()
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async login(input: LoginInput): Promise<AuthResponse> {
    try {
      const user = await this.circuitBreaker.execute(async () => {
        const foundUser = await this.userRepository.findByEmail(input.email);
        if (!foundUser) {
          throw new Error('INVALID_CREDENTIAL

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
Vou implementar uma aplicação React com TypeScript, sistema de design, hooks/services para APIs e componentes de dashboard interativos. Vou seguir rigorosamente as especificações do papel de Dev Frontend Sênior.

```bash
# Estrutura do projeto
diyapp-evolution-v12/
├── public/
├── src/
│   ├── components/
│   ├── hooks/

### `src/types/index.ts` - Tipos principais

```typescript
export interface User {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  email: string;
  avatar?: string;
  role: 'admin' | 'editor' | 'viewer';
  lastActive: string;
}

export interface Project {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  description: string;
  status: 'active' | 'archived' | 'completed';
  progress: number;
  dueDate: string;
  members: string[];
  createdAt: string;
}

export interface Task {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
  status: 'todo' | 'in-progress' | 'review' | 'done';
  priority: 'low' | 'medium' | 'high' | 'critical';
  assigneeId?: string;
  projectId: string;
  dueDate?: string;
  createdAt: string;
  updatedAt: string;
}

export interface Metric {
  id: string;
  label: string;
  value: number;
  change: number;
  changeType: 'increase' | 'decrease' | 'neutral';
  format: 'number' | 'percentage' | 'currency';
  currency?: string;
}

export interface ChartDataPoint {
  date: string;
  value: number;
  category?: string;
}

export interface ApiResponse<T> {
  data: T;
  success: boolean;
  message?: string;
  timestamp: string;
}

export interface ApiError {
  code: string;
  message: string;
  details?: Record<string, unknown>;
  timestamp: string;
}

export interface PaginatedResponse<T> {
  items: T[];
  total: number;
  page: number;
  limit: number;
  hasNext: boolean;
  hasPrev: boolean;
}

export type Theme = 'light' | 'dark';
```

import { ReactNode } from 'react';

export interface BaseComponentProps {
  className?: string;
  children?: ReactNode;
  'data-testid'?: string;
}

export interface CardProps extends BaseComponentProps {
  variant?: 'default' | 'elevated' | 'outlined';
  padding?: 'none' | 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
}

export interface ButtonProps extends BaseComponentProps {
  variant?: 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost' | 'danger';
  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
  isLoading?: boolean;
  disabled?: boolean;
  onClick?: () => void;
  type?: 'button' | 'submit' | 'reset';
  leftIcon?: ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: ReactNode;
}

export interface InputProps extends BaseComponentProps {
  type?: 'text' | 'email' | 'password' | 'number' | 'search';
  placeholder?: string;
  value?: string;
  defaultValue?: string;
  onChange?: (value: string) => void;
  error?: string;
  disabled?: boolean;
  required?: boolean;
  label?: string;
  helperText?: string;
}

export interface SelectOption {
  value: string;
  label: string;
  disabled?: boolean;
}

export interface SelectProps extends BaseComponentProps {
  options: SelectOption[];
  value?: string;
  defaultValue?: string;
  onChange?: (value: string) => void;
  placeholder?: string;
  disabled?: boolean;
  error?: string;

}

## 5. Utilitários

### `src/utils/format.ts` - Utilitários de formatação

```typescript
import { format, formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';
import { ptBR, enUS } from 'date-fns/locale';

export const formatDate = (date: string | Date, pattern = 'PP'): string => {
  const locale = navigator.language.startsWith('pt') ? ptBR : enUS;
  return format(new Date(date), pattern, { locale });
};

export const formatRelativeTime = (date: string | Date): string => {
  const locale = navigator.language.startsWith('pt') ? ptBR : enUS;
  return formatDistanceToNow(new Date(date), { addSuffix: true, locale });
};

export const formatCurrency = (
  value: number,
  currency = 'USD',
  locale = navigator.language
): string => {
  return new Intl.NumberFormat(locale, {
    style: 'currency',
    currency,
    minimumFractionDigits: 2,
    maximumFractionDigits: 2,
  }).format(value);
};

export const formatNumber = (
  value: number,
  options?: Intl.NumberFormatOptions
): string => {
  return new Intl.NumberFormat(navigator.language, options).format(value);
};

export const formatPercentage = (value: number): string => {
  return `${value > 0 ? '+' : ''}${value.toFixed(1)}%`;
};

export const truncateText = (text: string, maxLength: number): string => {
  if (text.length <= maxLength) return text;
  return `${text.slice(0, maxLength)}...`;
};
```

### `src/utils/validation.ts` - Validações

```typescript
export const validateEmail = (email: string): boolean => {
  const re = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/;
  return re.test(email);
};

export const validatePassword = (password: string): {
  isValid: boolean;
  errors: string[];
} => {
  const errors: string[] = [];
  
  if (password.length < 8) {
    errors.push('Password must be at least 8 characters long');
  }
  
  if (!/[A-Z]/.test(password)) {
    errors.push('Password must contain at least one uppercase letter');
  }
  
  if (!/[a-z]/.test(password)) {
    errors.push('Password must contain at least one lowercase letter');
  }
  
  if (!/\d/.test(password)) {
    errors.push('Password must contain at least one number');
  }
  
  if (!/[!@#$%^&*(),.?":{}|<>]/.test(password)) {
    errors.push('Password must contain at least one special character');
  }
  
  return {
    isValid: errors.length === 0,
    errors,
  };
};

export const validateRequired = (value: string): boolean => {
  return value.trim().length > 0;
};

export const validateUrl = (url: string): boolean => {
  try {
    new URL(url);
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
};
```



### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
```sql
-- ============================================
-- DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core
-- Database Schema & ETL Pipelines
-- Data Engineer: Senior Squad Member
-- ============================================

-- ============================================
-- 1. DATABASE SCHEMA (PostgreSQL 15+)
-- ============================================

-- ======================
-- 1.1 Core Tables (V12)
-- ======================

-- Users table with enhanced tracking
CREATE TABLE users_v12 (
    user_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    username VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    hashed_password VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    full_name VARCHAR(255),
    avatar_url TEXT,
    timezone VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'UTC',
    locale VARCHAR(10) DEFAULT 'en-US',
    
    -- Metadata
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    is_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    verification_token VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Analytics fields
    last_login_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    login_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    feature_flags JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    
    -- Indexes
    CONSTRAINT users_email_check CHECK (email ~* '^[A-Za-z0-9._%+-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.-]+\.[A-Za-z]{2,}$')
);

CREATE INDEX idx_users_email ON users_v12(email);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_created_at ON users_v12(created_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_active ON users_v12(is_active) WHERE is_active = TRUE;

-- Projects table
CREATE TABLE projects_v12 (
    project_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users_v12(user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    slug VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    
    -- Project configuration
    config JSONB DEFAULT '{
        "visibility": "private",
        "collaboration": false,
        "auto_save": true,
        "versioning": true
    }',
    
    -- Statistics
    file_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_size_bytes BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    last_modified_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Metadata
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    is_archived BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    
    -- Indexes
    CONSTRAINT projects_slug_check CHECK (slug ~* '^[a-z0-9]+(?:-[a-z0-9]+)*$')
);

CREATE INDEX idx_projects_user ON projects_v12(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_slug ON projects_v12(slug);
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_modified ON projects_v12(last_modified_at);

-- Files table with versioning
CREATE TABLE files_v12 (
    file_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES projects_v12(project_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    parent_file_id UUID REFERENCES files_v12(file_id),
    
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    path TEXT NOT NULL,
    file_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    mime_type VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Content storage (large files would use S3, but metadata here)
    content_hash VARCHAR(64), -- SHA-256
    content_size_bytes INTEGER,
    storage_location VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'database', -- 'database', 's3', 'local'
    storage_key TEXT,
    
    -- Versioning
    version INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
    is_current_version BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    previous_version_id UUID REFERENCES files_v12(file_id),
    
    -- Metadata
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    created_by UUID REFERENCES users_v12(user_id),
    updated_by UUID REFERENCES users_v12(user_id),
    
    -- Indexes
    UNIQUE(project_id, path, version)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_files_project ON files_v12(project_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_files_path ON files_v12(path);
CREATE INDEX idx_files_current_version ON files_v12(project_id, path) WHERE is_current_version = TRUE;

-- ======================
-- 1.2 Analytics Tables
-- ======================

-- User activity events (raw events)
CREATE TABLE raw_user_events (
    event_id BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    event_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users_v12(user_id),
    session_id VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Event data
    event_data JSONB NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Device/context info
    user_agent TEXT,
    ip_address INET,
    device_type VARCHAR(50),
    browser VARCHAR(100),
    os VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Processing flags
    processed BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    processed_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Indexes
    INDEX idx_raw_events_type_time ON raw_user_events(event_type, event_timestamp),
    INDEX idx_raw_events_user_time ON raw_user_events(user_id, event_timestamp),
    INDEX idx_raw_events_unprocessed ON raw_user_events(processed) WHERE processed = FALSE
);

-- Daily user metrics (aggregated)
CREATE TABLE daily_user_metrics (
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users_v12(user_id),
    
    -- Activity counts
    login_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    project_create_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    file_edit_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    api_call_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Session metrics
    total_session_duration_seconds INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    avg_session_duration_seconds INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Storage metrics
    total_storage_bytes BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    storage_change_bytes INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Performance metrics
    avg_response_time_ms INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    error_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Calculated fields
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    is_power_user BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    
    -- Metadata
    calculated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    PRIMARY KEY (date, user_id)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_daily_metrics_date ON daily_user_metrics(date);
CREATE INDEX idx_daily_metrics_user ON daily_user_metrics(user_id);

-- LLM usage tracking
CREATE TABLE llm_usage_metrics (
    metric_id BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    timestamp TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users_v12(user_id),
    project_id UUID REFERENCES projects_v12(project_id),
    
    -- LLM provider info
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- 'openai', 'anthropic', 'google'
    model VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, -- 'gpt-4', 'claude-3', etc
    endpoint VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, -- 'completion', 'chat', 'embeddings'
    
    -- Token usage
    prompt_tokens INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    completion_tokens INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_tokens INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Cost tracking (in USD)
    prompt_cost_usd DECIMAL(10, 6) DEFAULT 0,
    completion_cost_usd DECIMAL(10, 6) DEFAULT 0,
    total_cost_usd DECIMAL(10, 6) DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Performance
    response_time_ms INTEGER,
    success BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    error_message TEXT,
    
    -- Request metadata
    request_hash VARCHAR(64), -- For deduplication
    feature_name VARCHAR(100), -- Which feature used this
    
    -- Indexes
    INDEX idx_llm_usage_time ON llm_usage_metrics(timestamp),
    INDEX idx_llm_usage_user ON llm_usage_metrics(user_id),
    INDEX idx_llm_usage_provider_model ON llm_usage_metrics(provider, model)
);

-- ======================
-- 1.3 Cache Schema (Redis structure)
-- ======================

-- Note: This is documentation of Redis key patterns, not SQL

/*
REDIS KEY PATTERNS:

1. User sessions:
   session:{session_id} -> JSON with user data, permissions, TTL: 24h

2. Rate limiting:
   rate_limit:{user_id}:{endpoint} -> count, TTL: per window

3. Project cache:
   project:{project_id}:metadata -> JSON project data, TTL: 1h
   project:{project_id}:files -> Serialized file tree, TTL: 5m

4. File content cache:
   file:{file_id}:content:{hash} -> Compressed content, TTL: 15m

5. LLM response cache:
   llm_cache:{provider}:{model}:{hash} -> Cached response, TTL: 1h

6. Real-time notifications:
   user:{user_id}:notifications -> List of notifications

7. Analytics aggregation:
   metrics:daily:{date}:{metric} -> Aggregated value, TTL: 7d
*/

-- ============================================
-- 2. ETL PIPELINES (dbt models)
-- ============================================

-- models/staging/stg_raw_events.sql
WITH raw_events AS (
    SELECT
        event_id,
        event_type,
        user_id,
        session_id,
        event_data,
        event_timestamp,
        user_agent,
        ip_address,
        device_type,
        browser,
        os,
        processed,
        processed_at
    FROM raw_user_events
    WHERE event_timestamp >= DATE_TRUNC('day', CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '30 days')
)

SELECT
    event_id,
    event_type,
    user_id,
    session_id,
    
    -- Extract common fields from event_data
    event_data->>'path' as event_path,
    event_data->>'method' as http_method,
    event_data->>'status_code' as status_code,
    event_data->>'duration_ms' as duration_ms,
    event_data->>'error' as error_message,
    
    -- Parse user agent
    CASE
        WHEN user_agent ILIKE '%mobile%' THEN 'mobile'
        WHEN user_agent ILIKE '%tablet%' THEN 'tablet'
        ELSE 'desktop'
    END as device_category,
    
    browser,
    os,
    ip_address,
    
    -- Timestamps
    event_timestamp,
    DATE(event_timestamp) as event_date,
    EXTRACT(HOUR FROM event_timestamp) as event_hour,
    
    -- Processing flags
    processed,
    processed_at,
    
    -- Add hash for deduplication
    MD5(
        COALESCE(user_id::text, '') || 
        event_type || 
        event_timestamp::text || 
        COALESCE(event_data::text, '')
    ) as event_hash
    
FROM raw_events
WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;

-- models/staging/stg_llm_usage.sql
SELECT
    metric_id,
    timestamp,
    user_id,
    project_id,
    provider,
    model,
    endpoint,
    
    -- Token usage
    prompt_tokens,
    completion_tokens,
    total_tokens,
    
    -- Cost calculation (using provider rates)
    CASE provider
        WHEN 'openai' THEN 
            CASE model
                WHEN 'gpt-4' THEN prompt_tokens * 0.00003 + completion_tokens * 0.00006
                WHEN 'gpt-3.5-turbo' THEN prompt_tokens * 0.0000015 + completion_tokens * 0.000002
                ELSE prompt_tokens * 0.00001 + completion_tokens * 0.00003
            END
        WHEN 'anthropic' THEN 
            CASE model
                WHEN 'claude-3-opus' THEN prompt_tokens * 0.000015 + completion_tokens * 0.000075
                WHEN 'claude-3-sonnet' THEN prompt_tokens * 0.000003 + completion_tokens * 0.000015
                ELSE prompt_tokens * 0.000001 + completion_tokens * 0.000005
            END
        ELSE total_tokens * 0.000001
    END as calculated_cost_usd,
    
    -- Actual cost (if different)
    total_cost_usd,
    
    -- Performance
    response_time_ms,
    success,
    error_message,
    
    -- Request info
    request_hash,
    feature_name,
    
    -- Time dimensions
    DATE(timestamp) as usage_date,
    EXTRACT(HOUR FROM timestamp) as usage_hour,
    
    -- User classification
    CASE
        WHEN total_tokens > 10000 THEN 'high_usage'
        WHEN total_tokens > 1000 THEN 'medium_usage'
        ELSE 'low_usage'
    END as usage_tier
    
FROM llm_usage_metrics
WHERE timestamp >= DATE_TRUNC('month', CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '3 months');

-- models/marts/mart_daily_user_activity.sql
WITH daily_events AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(event_timestamp) as activity_date,
        user_id,
        
        -- Count events by type
        COUNT(*) as total_events,
        COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) as session_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN event_type = 'user_login' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as login_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN event_type = 'project_create' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as project_create_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN event_type = 'file_edit' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as file_edit_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN event_type LIKE 'api_%' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as api_call_count,
        
        -- Calculate session duration (simplified)
        MAX(CASE WHEN event_type = 'session_end' 
                THEN (event_data->>'duration_seconds')::INTEGER 
                ELSE 0 
             END) as total_session_seconds,
        
        -- Error rate
        SUM(CASE WHEN event_data->>'error' IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as error_count,
        
        -- Performance
        PERCENTILE_CONT(0.5) WITHIN GROUP (
            ORDER BY (event_data->>'duration_ms')::INTEGER
        ) as median_response_ms
        
    FROM {{ ref('stg_raw_events') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '90 days'
    GROUP BY 1, 2
),

llm_usage AS (
    SELECT
        usage_date,
        user_id,
        SUM(total_tokens) as total_tokens,
        SUM(calculated_cost_usd) as llm_cost_usd,
        COUNT(*) as llm_request_count
    FROM {{ ref('stg_llm_usage') }}
    GROUP BY 1, 2
),

storage_usage AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(updated_at) as usage_date,
        user_id,
        SUM(total_size_bytes) as total_storage_bytes
    FROM projects_v12
    WHERE deleted_at IS NULL
    GROUP BY 1, 2
)

SELECT
    COALESCE(e.activity_date, l.usage_date, s.usage_date) as metric_date,
    COALESCE(e.user_id, l.user_id, s.user_id) as user_id,
    
    -- Activity metrics
    COALESCE(e.total_events, 0) as total_events,
    COALESCE(e.session_count, 0) as session_count,
    COALESCE(e.login_count, 0) as login_count,
    COALESCE(e.project_create_count, 0) as project_create_count,
    COALESCE(e.file_edit_count, 0) as file_edit_count,
    COALESCE(e.api_call_count, 0) as api_call_count,
    
    -- Session metrics
    COALESCE(e.total_session_seconds, 0) as total_session_seconds,
    CASE 
        WHEN COALESCE(e.session_count, 0) > 0 
        THEN COALESCE(e.total_session_seconds, 0) / e.session_count 
        ELSE 0 
    END as avg_session_seconds,
    
    -- LLM metrics
    COALESCE(l.total_tokens, 0) as llm_total_tokens,
    COALESCE(l.llm_cost_usd, 0) as llm_cost_usd,
    COALESCE(l.llm_request_count, 0) as llm_request_count,
    
    -- Storage metrics
    COALESCE(s.total_storage_bytes, 0) as total_storage_bytes,
    
    -- Quality metrics
    COALESCE(e.error_count, 0) as error_count,
    CASE 
        WHEN COALESCE(e.total_events, 0) > 0 
        THEN e.error_count::DECIMAL / e.total_events 
        ELSE 0 
    END as error_rate,
    COALESCE(e.median_response_ms, 0) as median_response_ms,
    
    -- User classification
    CASE
        WHEN COALESCE(e.total_events, 0) >= 50 OR COALESCE(l.total_tokens, 0) >= 10000 THEN 'power_user'
        WHEN COALESCE(e.total_events, 0) >= 10 THEN 'active_user'
        ELSE 'casual_user'
    END as user_segment,
    
    -- Activity flags
    COALESCE(e.total_events, 0) > 0 as was_active,
    COALESCE(l.llm_request_count, 0) > 0 as used_llm,
    
    -- Metadata
    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP as calculated_at
    
FROM daily_events e
FULL OUTER JOIN llm_usage l 
    ON e.activity_date = l.usage_date AND e.user_id = l.user_id
FULL OUTER JOIN storage_usage s 
    ON COALESCE(e.activity_date, l.usage_date) = s.usage_date 
    AND COALESCE(e.user_id, l.user_id) = s.user_id;

-- ============================================

-- ============================================

-- Phase 1: Schema migration with zero downtime

-- Step 1: Create new tables alongside old ones
-- (Already done above with _v12 suffix)

-- Step 2: Create migration tracking table
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS migration_status (
    migration_id SERIAL

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core Architecture
Technical Architecture Specification for Autonomous Stability
"""

import os
import json
import yaml
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any
from enum import Enum
from datetime import datetime
import hashlib

# ============================================================================
# 1. ARCHITECTURE DECISION RECORDS (ADRs)
# ============================================================================

class ADRStatus(Enum):
    PROPOSED = "proposed"
    ACCEPTED = "accepted"
    DEPRECATED = "deprecated"
    SUPERSEDED = "superseded"

@dataclass
class ArchitectureDecision:
    id: str
    title: str
    date: str
    status: ADRStatus
    authors: List[str]
    context: str
    decision: str
    options: Dict[str, Dict[str, List[str]]]
    consequences: Dict[str, List[str]]
    review_date: Optional[str] = None
    
    def to_markdown(self) -> str:
        """Convert ADR to markdown format"""
        options_text = "\n".join([
            f"- **{name}**: {opt['description']}\n"
            f"  - ✅ {', '.join(opt.get('pros', []))}\n"
            f"  - ❌ {', '.join(opt.get('cons', []))}"
            for name, opt in self.options.items()
        ])
        
        return f"""# ADR-{self.id}: {self.title}

**Date**: {self.date}  
**Status**: {self.status.value.upper()}  
**Authors**: {', '.join(self.authors)}

## Context
{self.context}

## Decision
{self.decision}

## Options Considered
{options_text}

## Consequences
### Positive
{chr(10).join(f'- {c}' for c in self.consequences.get('positive', []))}

### Negative
{chr(10).join(f'- {c}' for c in self.consequences.get('negative', []))}

### Risks
{chr(10).join(f'- {c}' for c in self.consequences.get('risks', []))}

{"## Review Date: " + self.review_date if self.review_date else ""}
"""

class ADRRegistry:
    """Manages Architecture Decision Records"""
    
    def __init__(self, registry_path: str = "docs/adrs"):
        self.registry_path = registry_path
        os.makedirs(registry_path, exist_ok=True)
        self.decisions = self._load_existing_adrs()
    
    def _load_existing_adrs(self) -> Dict[str, ArchitectureDecision]:
        """Load existing ADRs from filesystem"""
        decisions = {}
        if os.path.exists(self.registry_path):
            for file in os.listdir(self.registry_path):
                if file.endswith(".md") and file.startswith("ADR-"):
                    with open(os.path.join(self.registry_path, file), 'r') as f:
                        content = f.read()
                        # Parse ADR from markdown (simplified)
                        decisions[file.replace(".md", "")] = content
        return decisions
    
    def create_adr(self, decision: ArchitectureDecision) -> str:
        """Create a new ADR"""
        filename = f"ADR-{decision.id}.md"
        filepath = os.path.join(self.registry_path, filename)
        
        with open(filepath, 'w') as f:
            f.write(decision.to_markdown())
        
        self.decisions[f"ADR-{decision.id}"] = decision.to_markdown()
        return filepath

# ============================================================================
# 2. MICROSERVICES ARCHITECTURE SPECIFICATION
# ============================================================================

class ServiceType(Enum):
    API_GATEWAY = "api-gateway"
    AUTH_SERVICE = "auth-service"
    USER_SERVICE = "user-service"
    TASK_SERVICE = "task-service"
    NOTIFICATION_SERVICE = "notification-service"
    LLM_ORCHESTRATOR = "llm-orchestrator"
    MONITORING_SERVICE = "monitoring-service"
    WORKFLOW_ENGINE = "workflow-engine"

@dataclass
class MicroserviceSpec:
    name: str
    service_type: ServiceType
    port: int
    health_check_path: str
    dependencies: List[ServiceType]
    resource_limits: Dict[str, str]
    environment_vars: Dict[str, str]
    replicas: int = 1
    version: str = "1.0.0"
    
    def to_docker_compose(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Convert to Docker Compose service definition"""
        return {
            "image": f"diyapp/{self.name}:{self.version}",
            "container_name": f"diyapp-{self.name}",
            "ports": [f"{self.port}:{self.port}"],
            "environment": self.environment_vars,
            "healthcheck": {
                "test": [f"curl -f http://localhost:{self.port}{self.health_check_path}"],
                "interval": "30s",
                "timeout": "10s",
                "retries": 3,
                "start_period": "40s"
            },
            "deploy": {
                "resources": {
                    "limits": self.resource_limits
                },
                "replicas": self.replicas
            },
            "networks": ["diyapp-network"]
        }

class ServiceMesh:
    """Service mesh configuration for microservices"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.services: Dict[ServiceType, MicroserviceSpec] = {}
        self.setup_default_services()
    
    def setup_default_services(self):
        """Setup default microservices for DIYAPP"""
        
        # API Gateway
        self.services[ServiceType.API_GATEWAY] = MicroserviceSpec(
            name="api-gateway",
            service_type=ServiceType.API_GATEWAY,
            port=8080,
            health_check_path="/health",
            dependencies=[],
            resource_limits={"cpus": "0.5", "memory": "512M"},
            environment_vars={
                "NODE_ENV": "production",
                "LOG_LEVEL": "info",
                "RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW": "900000",
                "RATE_LIMIT_MAX": "100"
            },
            replicas=2
        )
        
        # Authentication Service
        self.services[ServiceType.AUTH_SERVICE] = MicroserviceSpec(
            name="auth-service",
            service_type=ServiceType.AUTH_SERVICE,
            port=3001,
            health_check_path="/auth/health",
            dependencies=[],
            resource_limits={"cpus": "0.3", "memory": "256M"},
            environment_vars={
                "JWT_SECRET": "${JWT_SECRET}",
                "JWT_EXPIRY": "24h",
                "REDIS_URL": "redis://redis:6379"
            }
        )
        
        # LLM Orchestrator Service
        self.services[ServiceType.LLM_ORCHESTRATOR] = MicroserviceSpec(
            name="llm-orchestrator",
            service_type=ServiceType.LLM_ORCHESTRATOR,
            port=3004,
            health_check_path="/llm/health",
            dependencies=[ServiceType.TASK_SERVICE],
            resource_limits={"cpus": "1.0", "memory": "2G"},
            environment_vars={
                "OPENAI_API_KEY": "${OPENAI_API_KEY}",
                "ANTHROPIC_API_KEY": "${ANTHROPIC_API_KEY}",
                "LLM_CACHE_TTL": "3600",
                "MAX_TOKENS": "4000"
            },
            replicas=3
        )
        
        # Monitoring Service
        self.services[ServiceType.MONITORING_SERVICE] = MicroserviceSpec(
            name="monitoring-service",
            service_type=ServiceType.MONITORING_SERVICE,
            port=9090,
            health_check_path="/metrics",
            dependencies=[],
            resource_limits={"cpus": "0.2", "memory": "512M"},
            environment_vars={
                "PROMETHEUS_MULTIPROC_DIR": "/tmp",
                "METRICS_PORT": "9090"
            }
        )
    
    def generate_docker_compose(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Generate complete docker-compose.yml"""
        services = {}
        for spec in self.services.values():
            services[spec.name] = spec.to_docker_compose()
        
        # Add supporting services
        services["redis"] = {
            "image": "redis:7-alpine",
            "container_name": "diyapp-redis",
            "ports": ["6379:6379"],
            "volumes": ["redis-data:/data"],
            "command": "redis-server --appendonly yes",
            "networks": ["diyapp-network"]
        }
        
        services["postgres"] = {
            "image": "postgres:15-alpine",
            "container_name": "diyapp-postgres",
            "ports": ["5432:5432"],
            "environment": {
                "POSTGRES_DB": "diyapp",
                "POSTGRES_USER": "diyapp",
                "POSTGRES_PASSWORD": "${DB_PASSWORD}"
            },
            "volumes": ["postgres-data:/var/lib/postgresql/data"],
            "networks": ["diyapp-network"]
        }
        
        return {
            "version": "3.8",
            "services": services,
            "volumes": {
                "redis-data": None,
                "postgres-data": None
            },
            "networks": {
                "diyapp-network": {
                    "driver": "bridge"
                }
            }
        }

# 4. CI/CD PIPELINE CONFIGURATION

class CICDPipeline:
    """CI/CD Pipeline configuration for autonomous deployment"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def generate_github_workflows() -> Dict[str, str]:
        """Generate GitHub Actions workflows"""
        
        # Main CI workflow
        ci_workflow = """name: CI Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main, develop ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main, develop ]

jobs:
  lint-and-test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    strategy:
      matrix:
        node-version: [18.x]
        python-version: [3.11]
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Setup Node.js
      uses: actions/setup-node@v3
      with:
        node-version: \${{ matrix.node-version }}
        cache: 'npm'
    
    - name: Setup Python
      uses: actions/setup-python@v4
      with:
        python-version: \${{ matrix.python-version }}
    
    - name: Install dependencies
      run: |
        npm ci
        pip install -r requirements.txt
        pip install -r requirements-dev.txt
    
    - name: Lint TypeScript
      run: npm run lint
    
    - name: Lint Python
      run: |
        black --check src/
        flake8 src/
        mypy src/
    
    - name: Run tests with coverage
      run: |
        npm test -- --coverage
        pytest --cov=src --cov-report=xml
    
    - name: Upload coverage to Codecov
      uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
      with:
        files: ./coverage.xml,./coverage/lcov.info
        fail_ci_if_error: true
    
    - name: Security scan
      uses: snyk/actions/node@master
      env:
        SNYK_TOKEN: \${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
      with:
        args: --severity-threshold=high
    
    - name: Build Docker images
      run: |
        docker build -t diyapp-api:latest -f Dockerfile.api .
        docker build -t diyapp-worker:latest -f Dockerfile.worker .

  integration-tests:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: lint-and-test
    services:
      postgres:
        image: postgres:15-alpine
        env:
          POSTGRES_PASSWORD: postgres
        options: >-
          --health-cmd pg_isready
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
      redis:
        image: redis:7-alpine
        options: >-
          --health-cmd "redis-cli ping"
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Run integration tests
      env:
        DATABASE_URL: postgresql://postgres:postgres@postgres:5432/test_db
        REDIS_URL: redis://redis:6379
      run: |
        npm run test:integration
        pytest tests/integration/
"""
        
        # CD workflow
        cd_workflow = """name: CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
    tags: [ 'v*' ]

jobs:
  deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: github.event_name == 'push' && github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Configure AWS credentials
      uses: aws-actions/configure-aws-credentials@v2
      with:
        aws-access-key-id: \${{ secrets.AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID }}
        aws-secret-access-key: \${{ secrets.AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY }}
        aws-region: \${{ vars.AWS_REGION }}
    
    - name: Login to Amazon ECR
      id: login-ecr
      uses: aws-actions/amazon-ecr-login@v1
    
    - name: Build, tag, and push images
      env:
        ECR_REGISTRY: \${{ steps.login-ecr.outputs.registry }}
        ECR_REPOSITORY: diyapp
        IMAGE_TAG: \${{ github.sha }}
      run: |
        docker build -t \$ECR_REGISTRY/\$ECR_REPOSITORY/api:\$IMAGE_TAG -f Dockerfile.api .
        docker build -t \$ECR_REGISTRY/\

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Sistema de Design

Vou criar um sistema de design completo com tokens, componentes atômicos e protótipos interativos para o DIYAPP V12.

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="pt-BR">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>DIYAPP V12 - Design System</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.4.0/css/all.min.css">
    <style>
        /* ===== DESIGN TOKENS ===== */
        :root {
            /* Cores primárias - Baseadas em WCAG AA */
            --color-primary-50: #f0f9ff;
            --color-primary-100: #e0f2fe;
            --color-primary-200: #bae6fd;
            --color-primary-300: #7dd3fc;
            --color-primary-400: #38bdf8;
            --color-primary-500: #0ea5e9;
            --color-primary-600: #0284c7;
            --color-primary-700: #0369a1;
            --color-primary-800: #075985;
            --color-primary-900: #0c4a6e;
            
            /* Cores neutras - Contraste garantido */
            --color-neutral-50: #fafafa;
            --color-neutral-100: #f5f5f5;
            --color-neutral-200: #e5e5e5;
            --color-neutral-300: #d4d4d4;
            --color-neutral-400: #a3a3a3;
            --color-neutral-500: #737373;
            --color-neutral-600: #525252;

// 3. src/config/index.ts
import dotenv from 'dotenv';
import { z } from 'zod';

dotenv.config();

const configSchema = z.object({
  NODE_ENV: z.enum(['development', 'production', 'test']).default('development'),
  PORT: z.string().transform(Number).default('3000'),
  
  // Database
  DB_HOST: z.string().default('localhost'),
  DB_PORT: z.string().transform(Number).default('5432'),
  DB_NAME: z.string().default('diyapp_v12'),
  DB_USER: z.string().default('postgres'),
  DB_PASSWORD: z.string().default('postgres'),
  
  // JWT
  JWT_SECRET: z.string().min(32),
  JWT_EXPIRES_IN: z.string().default('24h'),
  JWT_REFRESH_SECRET: z.string().min(32),
  JWT_REFRESH_EXPIRES_IN: z.string().default('7d'),
  
  // Redis
  REDIS_HOST: z.string().default('localhost'),
  REDIS_PORT: z.string().transform(Number).default('6379'),
  REDIS_PASSWORD: z.string().optional(),
  
  // Message Broker
  RABBITMQ_URL: z.string().default('amqp://localhost:5672'),
  KAFKA_BROKERS: z.string().default('localhost:9092'),
  
  // Rate Limiting
  RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS: z.string().transform(Number).default('900000'), // 15 minutes
  RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS: z.string().transform(Number).default('100'),
  
  // External Services
  EXTERNAL_API_TIMEOUT_MS: z.string().transform(Number).default('5000'),
  EXTERNAL_API_RETRY_ATTEMPTS: z.string().transform(Number).default('3'),
  
  // Observability
  LOG_LEVEL: z.enum(['error', 'warn', 'info', 'debug']).default('info'),
  METRICS_PORT: z.string().transform(Number).default('9090'),
  
  // Security
  CORS_ORIGIN: z.string().default('*'),
  TRUST_PROXY: z.string().transform(Boolean).default('false'),
});

export type Config = z.infer<typeof configSchema>;

export const config: Config = configSchema.parse(process.env);

// 4. src/utils/logger.ts
import winston from 'winston';
import { config } from '../config';

const { combine, timestamp, json, errors } = winston.format;

export const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: config.LOG_LEVEL,
  format: combine(
    errors({ stack: true }),
    timestamp(),
    json()
  ),
  defaultMeta: { service: 'diyapp-v12-core' },
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console(),
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: 'logs/error.log', 
      level: 'error',
      maxsize: 5242880, // 5MB
      maxFiles: 5,
    }),
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: 'logs/combined.log',
      maxsize: 5242880,
      maxFiles: 5,
    }),
  ],
});

// Correlation ID middleware
import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid';

export const correlationIdMiddleware = (
  req: Request,
  res: Response,
  next: NextFunction
): void => {
  const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] as string || uuidv4();
  res.setHeader('x-correlation-id', correlationId);
  
  // Add to request for use in services
  req.correlationId = correlationId;
  
  // Create child logger with correlation ID
  req.logger = logger.child({ correlationId });
  
  next();
};

// 5. src/utils/errors.ts
export class AppError extends Error {
  constructor(
    public message: string,
    public statusCode: number = 500,
    public isOperational: boolean = true,
    public details?: Record<string, any>
  ) {
    super(message);
    Object.setPrototypeOf(this, AppError.prototype);
    Error.captureStackTrace(this, this.constructor);
  }
}

export class ValidationError extends AppError {
  constructor(message: string, details?: Record<string, any>) {
    super(message, 400, true, details);
  }
}

export class AuthenticationError extends AppError {
  constructor(message: string = 'Authentication required') {
    super(message, 401);
  }
}

export class AuthorizationError extends AppError {
  constructor(message: string = 'Insufficient permissions') {
    super(message, 403);
  }
}

export class NotFoundError extends AppError {
  constructor(resource: string = 'Resource') {
    super(`${resource} not found`, 404);
  }
}

export class ConflictError extends AppError {
  constructor(message: string = 'Resource conflict') {
    super(message, 409);
  }
}

export class RateLimitError extends AppError {
  constructor(message: string = 'Rate limit exceeded') {
    super(message, 429);
  }
}

// 6. src/utils/resilience.ts
import CircuitBreaker from 'circuit-breaker-js';

export interface ExternalServiceConfig {
  name: string;
  timeoutMs: number;
  maxRetries: number;
  circuitBreakerThreshold: number;
  circuitBreakerDuration: number;
}

export class ResilientClient {
  private circuitBreakers: Map<string, CircuitBreaker> = new Map();
  
  constructor(private config: ExternalServiceConfig) {
    this.initializeCircuitBreaker();
  }
  
  private initializeCircuitBreaker(): void {
    const cb = new CircuitBreaker({
      windowDuration: 10000,
      numBuckets: 10,
      timeoutDuration: this.config.timeoutMs,
      errorThreshold: this.config.circuitBreakerThreshold,
      volumeThreshold: 10,
    });
    
    this.circuitBreakers.set(this.config.name, cb);
  }
  
  async execute<T>(
    operation: () => Promise<T>,
    fallback?: () => Promise<T>
  ): Promise<T> {
    const circuitBreaker = this.circuitBreakers.get(this.config.name);
    
    if (!circuitBreaker) {
      throw new Error(`Circuit breaker not initialized for ${this.config.name}`);
    }
    
    if (!circuitBreaker.allowRequest()) {
      // Circuit is open
      if (fallback) {
        return await fallback();
      }
      throw new Error(`Service ${this.config.name} is unavailable (circuit open)`);
    }
    
    let attempts = 0;
    
    while (attempts <= this.config.maxRetries) {
      try {
        const result = await Promise.race([
          operation(),
          new Promise<never>((_, reject) => {
            setTimeout(() => reject(new Error(`Timeout after ${this.config.timeoutMs}ms`)), 
                     this.config.timeoutMs);
          })
        ]);
        
        circuitBreaker.success();
        return result;
      } catch (error) {
        attempts++;
        
        // Only retry on timeout or 5xx errors
        const shouldRetry = 
          error.message.includes('Timeout') ||
          (error.response?.status >= 500 && error.response?.status < 600);
        
        if (attempts > this.config.maxRetries || !shouldRetry) {
          circuitBreaker.failure();
          
          if (fallback) {
            return await fallback();
          }
          
          throw error;
        }
        
        // Exponential backoff with jitter
        const delay = Math.min(1000 * Math.pow(2, attempts) + Math.random() * 100, 10000);
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));
      }
    }
    
    throw new Error(`Max retries (${this.config.maxRetries}) exceeded for ${this.config.name}`);
  }
}

// 7. src/database/entities/user.entity.ts
import { Entity, PrimaryGeneratedColumn, Column, CreateDateColumn, UpdateDateColumn, Index } from 'typeorm';

@Entity('users')
export class User {
  @PrimaryGeneratedColumn('uuid')
  id!: string;

  @Column({ unique: true })
  @Index()
  email!: string;

  @Column()
  passwordHash!: string;

  @Column({ nullable: true })
  fullName?: string;

  @Column({ default: false })
  isEmailVerified!: boolean;

  @Column({ default: 'user' })
  role!: string; // 'user', 'admin', 'moderator'

  @Column({ type: 'jsonb', nullable: true })
  metadata?: Record<string, any>;

  @Column({ nullable: true })
  lastLoginAt?: Date;

  @CreateDateColumn()
  createdAt!: Date;

  @UpdateDateColumn()
  updatedAt!: Date;

  // Soft delete
  @Column({ nullable: true })
  deletedAt?: Date;
}

// 8. src/database/entities/task.entity.ts
import { Entity, PrimaryGeneratedColumn, Column, CreateDateColumn, UpdateDateColumn, ManyToOne, JoinColumn, Index } from 'typeorm';
import { User } from './user.entity';

export enum TaskStatus {
  PENDING = 'pending',
  PROCESSING = 'processing',
  COMPLETED = 'completed',
  FAILED = 'failed',
  CANCELLED = 'cancelled'
}

export enum TaskPriority {
  LOW = 'low',
  MEDIUM = 'medium',
  HIGH = 'high',
  CRITICAL = 'critical'
}

@Entity('tasks')
export class Task {
  @PrimaryGeneratedColumn('uuid')
  id!: string;

  @Column()
  type!: string; // 'email', 'notification', 'report', 'sync', etc.

  @Column({ type: 'jsonb' })
  payload!: Record<string, any>;

  @Column({ type: 'jsonb', nullable: true })
  result?: Record<string, any>;

  @Column({ type: 'enum', enum: TaskStatus, default: TaskStatus.PENDING })
  status!: TaskStatus;

  @Column({ type: 'enum', enum: TaskPriority, default: TaskPriority.MEDIUM })
  priority!: TaskPriority;

  @Column({ nullable: true })
  scheduledFor?: Date;

  @Column({ nullable: true })
  startedAt?: Date;

  @Column({ nullable: true })
  completedAt?: Date;

  @Column({ nullable: true })
  errorMessage?: string;

  @Column({ type: 'int', default: 0 })
  retryCount!: number;

  @Column({ type: 'int', default: 3 })
  maxRetries!: number;

  @ManyToOne(() => User, { nullable: true })
  @JoinColumn({ name: 'userId' })
  user?: User;

  @Column({ nullable: true })
  userId?: string;

  @CreateDateColumn()
  createdAt!: Date;

  @UpdateDateColumn()
  updatedAt!: Date;

  @Column({ type: 'jsonb', nullable: true })
  metadata?: Record<string, any>;
}

        id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
        email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
        password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
        full_name VARCHAR(255),

        payload JSONB NOT NULL,

      );

      CREATE INDEX idx_tasks_priority ON tasks(priority);
      CREATE INDEX idx_tasks_scheduled_for ON tasks(scheduled_for);
      CREATE INDEX idx_tasks_user_id ON tasks(user_id);
      CREATE INDEX idx_tasks_created_at ON tasks(created_at);
    `);
  }

  public async down(queryRunner: QueryRunner): Promise<void> {
    await queryRunner.query(`DROP TABLE IF EXISTS tasks;`);
    await queryRunner.query(`DROP TABLE IF EXISTS users;`);
  }
}

// src/design-system/ThemeProvider.tsx
import React, { createContext, useContext } from 'react';

// Tokens do Design System - NUNCA valores hardcoded
export const tokens = {
  colors: {
    primary: {
      50: '#f0f9ff',
      100: '#e0f2fe',
      500: '#0ea5e9',
      600: '#0284c7',
      700: '#0369a1',
    },
    neutral: {
      50: '#fafafa',
      100: '#f5f5f5',
      200: '#e5e5e5',
      300: '#d4d4d4',
      700: '#404040',
      800: '#262626',
      900: '#171717',
    },
    semantic: {
      success: '#10b981',
      warning: '#f59e0b',
      error: '#ef4444',
      info: '#3b82f6',
    },
  },
  spacing: {
    xs: '0.25rem', // 4px
    sm: '0.5rem',  // 8px
    md: '1rem',    // 16px
    lg: '1.5rem',  // 24px
    xl: '2rem',    // 32px
    '2xl': '3rem', // 48px
  },
  typography: {
    fontFamily: {
      sans: "'Inter', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, sans-serif",
      mono: "'JetBrains Mono', 'Courier New', monospace",
    },
    fontSize: {
      xs: '0.75rem',   // 12px
      sm: '0.875rem',  // 14px
      base: '1rem',    // 16px
      lg: '1.125rem',  // 18px
      xl: '1.25rem',   // 20px
      '2xl': '1.5rem', // 24px
      '3xl': '1.875rem', // 30px
    },
    fontWeight: {
      normal: '400',
      medium: '500',
      semibold: '600',
      bold: '700',
    },
  },
  borderRadius: {
    sm: '0.25rem', // 4px
    md: '0.375rem', // 6px
    lg: '0.5rem',   // 8px
    xl: '0.75rem',  // 12px
    full: '9999px',
  },
  shadows: {
    sm: '0 1px 2px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.05)',
    md: '0 4px 6px -1px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
    lg: '0 10px 15px -3px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
  },
  zIndex: {
    dropdown: 1000,
    modal: 2000,
    tooltip: 3000,
  },
} as const;

export type ThemeTokens = typeof tokens;

const ThemeContext = createContext<ThemeTokens>(tokens);

export const useTheme = () => {
  const context = useContext(ThemeContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error('useTheme must be used within ThemeProvider');
  }
  return context;
};

interface ThemeProviderProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

export const ThemeProvider: React.FC<ThemeProviderProps> = ({ children }) => {
  // Injetar fontes do Google Fonts
  React.useEffect(() => {
    const link = document.createElement('link');
    link.href = 'https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@400;500;600;700&family=JetBrains+Mono&display=swap';
    link.rel = 'stylesheet';
    document.head.appendChild(link);
    
    return () => {
      document.head.removeChild(link);
    };
  }, []);

  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider value={tokens}>
      <div style={{ fontFamily: tokens.typography.fontFamily.sans }}>
        {children}
      </div>
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
};
